Current Commentary

Can the United States and Great Britain Cooperate?

— A Discussion

The clamor for cooperation between the United States and Great Britain has been going on for a long time. The intermittent news and the intricate problems have made it difficult for those who pay attention to current affairs to grasp the situation. Recently, the Far East issue has suddenly become tense, and the international peace movement has gradually gained attention from academic and public opinion circles in various countries. As a result, the theory of US-British cooperation has once again become rife. According to National News Agency reports, Washington publicly declared on the 14th of this month that "the United States and Great Britain are about to implement close cooperation to maintain world peace, and the substance of this cooperation will be more powerful than at any time in recent years," and so on.

Cooperation between the United States and Great Britain is certainly welcome. The success of US-British cooperation would also be enough to reverse the current international situation. However, after reviewing historical facts, I feel that the opposition between the United States and Great Britain has already become a fundamental opposition in present-day capitalism. At a time when the clamor for narrow nationalism is rising to the clouds, whether the United States and Great Britain can sincerely cooperate to maintain international peace is doubtful. Let's discuss it further.

First, in terms of economics, since the failure of the World Economic Conference, the contradictions between the United States and Great Britain have already embarked on an irreconcilable path. The war debt issue has not been resolved for a long time, and the struggle for currency devaluation has arisen again. In addition, raising tariff barriers and closing commodity and raw material markets have only worsened the trade competition between the two countries. Currently, the United States and Great Britain are in direct or indirect conflict in the markets of China, Australia, India, Canada, and Latin American countries, both in terms of trade and investment. The intensification of this kind of market competition is intensifying the currency war and deepening the contradictions between the two countries.

Second, in terms of politics, the deterioration of the economic opposition between the two countries will inevitably form a basis for political disagreement. The open and secret political struggles between the United States and Great Britain are almost constant. They have failed to reach a consensus on the Far East issue and are engaging in schemes to manipulate Latin America and Canada politically. Although the United States ostensibly adheres to the principle of non-interference on European issues, in reality, it still intends to wait for an opportunity to act, which forces Great Britain to be wary.

Third, in terms of military preparedness, Great Britain's claim is to maintain its traditional maritime hegemony, while the United States' position is to complete its most advantageous naval plan. Last year, during the preparatory meeting for the London Naval Conference, Great Britain's total tonnage principle and the United States' big ship and big gun policy almost came to blows, which ultimately led to the indefinite postponement of the Naval Conference and the open fact of naval arms race among the nations.

The above points are all major ones. From this, it can be seen that the road to US-British cooperation is full of hidden reefs. There can be no fundamental success unless both countries abandon their self-centered positions.

However, although fundamental cooperation between the United States and Great Britain is impossible to realize, partial cooperation may not be seen as a matter of fact. From our observation, there are two possibilities for US-British partial cooperation. One is the growing crisis of East Asian monopoly, and the other is the increasing "global dumping" of Japanese goods, which poses a serious threat to the inherent markets of the United States and Great Britain. This kind of economic conflict with Japan has now become increasingly fierce, so the United States and Great Britain will eventually take a consistent step on a common ground.

Page 8

Abyssinian Issue: Italian Attitude Softens; No Longer Opposes League of Nations Intervention; British and French Steps Tend Toward Consensus; Current Problem Centers on Right of Way

(Paris) In the next few days, the atmosphere surrounding the Italo-Ethiopian dispute is expected to improve significantly. Reuters has learned that this change will come from Italy's softening of its opposition to League of Nations intervention. The French government seems to have taken a firm approach, supporting mediation by Geneva, as requested by British Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval. Diplomatic sources in Rome say that all signs are quite favorable. (17th Reuters Dispatch)

(Geneva) League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol today telegraphed member states of the Executive Council, preparing to attend a special meeting from July 25 to August 2 to consider the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. The telegram explicitly stated that the League of Nations will consider intervening in this matter. (17th National Dispatch)

(Paris) The talk that the League of Nations will convene a meeting on July 25 to discuss the Italo-Ethiopian dispute is gaining momentum. League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol met with Prime Minister Laval this afternoon. Well-informed sources claim that the two discussed the Italo-Ethiopian issue and the League of Nations Executive Council's convening of a meeting on July 25. It is increasingly believed here that the best way to resolve the dispute is to allow the League of Nations to implement its resolution passed in May, even if it provokes the indignation of various countries over Italy's policies, and causes other consequences. (17th National Dispatch)

(Rome) It is reported that the Ethiopian Emperor is willing to cede part of the Wogadan province to Italy. The Italian authorities have sternly refused to consider this proposal, claiming that Wogadan province is a desert and completely unsuitable for colonization. Well-informed sources now say that the railway connecting Eritrea and Italian Somaliland will be dangerous and useless unless it is occupied by troops. British Ambassador to Rome Sir Drummond has met with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini again today. (18th Reuters Dispatch)

(London) Since the Emperor of Abyssinia requested the United States to intervene in the Italo-Ethiopian dispute based on the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the United States politely declined, the United States and Great Britain are discussing the Abyssinian issue through diplomatic channels. It is generally believed that although the United States admits that it has no obligation to intervene, its main goal is to assist Great Britain's mediation efforts so that the Italo-Ethiopian dispute can be resolved. Well-informed sources believe that the US government may send observers to Geneva. (17th Havas Dispatch)

Ethiopian Emperor Declares: Hopes League of Nations Handles; Will Not Make Diplomatic Contacts Beforehand

(London) The Emperor of Abyssinia gave an interview to a reporter from the Times yesterday, explaining the country's views on the current state of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. He said, "Ethiopia hopes that the League of Nations Executive Council can discuss this dispute on July 25. Before the Executive Council makes a decision, no diplomatic activities will be undertaken. If the Italo-Ethiopian Mixed Arbitration Committee can reconvene before July 25, Ethiopia will naturally await the results and intends to propose a new procedure. If Great Britain directly makes any suggestions to Ethiopia, Ethiopia is willing to respond. Regarding the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, Ethiopia truly regards the treaty signed by Great Britain, France, and Italy in 1906 as a tool for maintaining peace. However, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's continued troop deployments and arms shipments, and the talk that he himself may come to East Africa, make it impossible to implement the revised treaty of 1906, even if one wishes to. Moreover, is only Great Britain supporting this treaty? As for the manner of conducting negotiations, no suggestions have been made by any party. Ethiopia truly approves of the attitudes of British Foreign Secretary Hoare and Minister without Portfolio Eden. Ethiopia does not object to Great Britain's desire to maintain freedom of action in order to contribute to the establishment of peace. As for the construction of a railway through Ethiopia from Italian Eritrea to Italian Somaliland, the Italian government has not made this proposal, nor has any other government made this claim. The Ethiopian government is still willing to discuss this issue." Regarding the issue of ceding territory, the Ethiopian Emperor's attitude is very clear, believing that exchanging territory is acceptable, but Ethiopia will never recognize ceding territory alone, saying, "If Great Britain is still willing to give the port of Zeila to Ethiopia, then Ethiopia will cede equal land to Italy, but the location of this territory has not been decided. In short, the territory on the northern border of Ethiopia will never be ceded." According to reports, when the Ethiopian Emperor last toured Europe, he expressed the necessity for the country to obtain a port on the Red Sea. Now, he said that this issue is of particular importance to Ethiopia. The Emperor finally said, "Italy's threat to peace is already obvious. If the country declares war on Ethiopia and sends its troops into Ethiopian territory, the Ethiopian government will immediately fight back on the one hand and appeal to the League of Nations on the other." (18th Havas Dispatch)

Cairo: Local Arabic newspapers published excerpts from the Ethiopian Emperor's statements, saying that if Egypt allows Italian military aircraft to cross Egyptian territory, he will consider this an unfriendly act, as it facilitates Italy's activities in invading Ethiopia. Ethiopia still hopes to resolve this dispute peacefully, but is also prepared to exert all its strength to maintain its national independence. (18th Reuters Dispatch)

(Paris) According to Madame de Thubali, the diplomatic correspondent for L'Oeuvre, League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol's proposal for the British and French governments to hold a tripartite meeting with Italy to discuss the Italo-Ethiopian issue has failed. Thubali also said that this proposal could have been accepted by France, but because of the attitudes of Great Britain and Italy, it ultimately became a pie in the sky. The British government still requires the dispute to be submitted to the League of Nations for resolution. Therefore, the League of Nations Executive Council's convening of a meeting on July 25 is unavoidable. The French ambassador to Italy's inquiry into the true intentions of the Italian side was also ineffective. Prime Minister Mussolini only said that he wanted to safeguard Italy's dignity and had no other choice but to attack Ethiopia, refusing to make any further statements. Mussolini is unwilling to continue negotiations, but may eventually accept a reconciliation. In order for Italy to utilize the League of Nations, Thubali advocates that Italy should submit evidence to the League of Nations to prove that its accusations against Ethiopia, such as violating treaties and engaging in the slave trade, are indeed facts. (18th National Dispatch)

Mussolini Indicates Will Use Force From Beginning to End; Rome Releases New Account of Events

Milan: Prime Minister Mussolini wrote an article today in Il Popolo d'Italia, the newspaper he founded, saying that the Italo-Ethiopian dispute "began with force and must end with force." (17th National Dispatch)

(Rome) On May 31, a group of Ethiopian natives attacked the Italian army defense line in Tangari, on the border of Italian Eritrea, leading to a new dispute. The official statement of the details of this case is as follows: on the night of that day, Ethiopians belonging to the "Damo Sita" and "Ale Da" tribes, and from the highlands, crossed the border and suddenly invaded the "Matra" plain in Italian Eritrea, and attacked the local Italian tribes. Upon hearing the news, the Italian army immediately rushed to the scene and repelled the Ethiopians. In this battle, many herders, women, and children were killed by the Ethiopian natives, and 4,000 heads of livestock and some people were looted and taken away as slaves. When the Italian army stationed in Sabog Port received the report, it sent a team to the scene of the incident, but the Ethiopian natives had already fled far across the border. (18th Havas Dispatch)

British Military Preparations to Protect African Territories; But No Need to Increase Military Strength

(London) Colonial Secretary Malcolm MacDonald told the House of Commons today that if Italy and Ethiopia go to war, Great Britain is prepared to protect the borders of its African territories. He said that the troop movements in the Ganze area were to prevent accidents, but there was no need to increase military strength in the territories. (17th National Dispatch)

(London) The House of Lords convened a meeting to discuss the Abyssinian slavery system based on the League of Nations reports. Lord Cecil, Lord Buxton, and Archbishop of Canterbury spoke successively, explaining the slow progress of Abyssinia in abolishing the slavery system, expressing praise for the efforts made by the Ethiopian Emperor. Lord Buxton explained that the existence of slavery in Abyssinia "cannot be used as a pretext for invading Abyssinia." (17th Havas Dispatch)

League of Nations Sanctions Issue; Committee Prepares Report

(Geneva) The League of Nations Executive Council's small committee on economic sanctions has completed its discussion and drafted a report, which can be submitted to the Committee of Thirteen. The purpose of the committee is to increase the effectiveness of the collective security system. The committee will meet on July 24 to discuss the recommendations in the report. The report analyzes prevention plans and the implementation of sanctions very clearly, recognizing that prohibiting the trafficking and manufacturing of raw materials used for armaments is a prevention plan, while actual sanctions may completely sever trade relations with the violating country. However, this universal ban should not be applied to goods necessary for human nutrition. The report also states that some countries may not participate in these sanctions, so it is necessary to find ways to prevent these neutral countries from supplying the violating country with arms and raw materials. The small committee itself has some doubts about whether its recommendations can be effective. The report concludes that the various recommendations put forward may cause all sorts of problems, but this is enough to prove the difficulty of the small committee's work. (15th National Dispatch)

Royal Yacht Guides Fleet in Simulated Naval Battle; Merchant Fleet Participates in Exercise for the First Time

(London) Today, the King, aboard his royal yacht, guided the fleet in a simulated naval battle. One of the unique aspects of this exercise was the use of specially designed shells by the cruisers to bombard radio-controlled target ships. These shells shattered upon impact. Following this, four of the largest battleships, with twenty large cannons of [unclear, illegible character] feet, bombarded a target ship traveling at twenty nautical miles per hour. Additionally, several aircraft, controlled by radio, launched fierce bombardments against the warships, which retaliated with [unclear, illegible character] anti-aircraft fire. Several torpedo boats [unclear, illegible character] bombarded the cruiser "Nelson," but were repelled by cannon and machine gun fire. After the exercise, the entire fleet sailed past the royal yacht, on which the King was [unclear, illegible character]. The officers and men on the ships cheered in salute as they passed the royal yacht. [unclear, illegible character] Chamberlain immediately received a handwritten message from the King, expressing his satisfaction with the naval exercise and commending all the naval officers and men. He also expressed his pleasure with the first-time participation of the merchant fleet in the exercise. (Reuters, 17th)

(London) King George V this morning [unclear, illegible character] inspected the navy at Portsmouth Naval Dockyard. During the shooting exercise, the fleet bombardment of automated aircraft was demonstrated for the first time. The method involved [unclear, illegible character] two aircraft, which were first launched into the sky using projectors, [unclear, illegible character] then controlled remotely via radio, allowing them to freely [unclear, illegible character] soar. One of the aircraft crashed before it could ascend, [unclear, illegible character] while the other flew back and forth, appearing quite natural. Consequently, the ships opened fire [unclear, illegible character] . Finally, the armored ship "Rodney" hit the upper wing of the aircraft with its anti-aircraft guns, causing it to crash. In addition, a simulated bombardment of a cruiser was demonstrated. [unclear, illegible character] The method involved using the cruiser "Vindictive," also controlled via radio, as a target for the ships to fire at. A total of 220 shots were fired, of which 56 hit the hull of the "Vindictive." (Havas, 17th)

France Vigorously Implements Austerity Measures; Opinions Vary Among Factions; Large Problems for Civil Servants; Laval Delivers Radio Address

(Paris) Following the government's announcement of austerity orders to save substantial funds and balance the budget, a sense of optimism has returned to the country. The stock exchange, most sensitive to public sentiment, has shown a positive reaction. Government bonds have soared in price, as the nation's financial position is expected to improve. However, shares in electricity, mining, munitions, and real estate companies have all fallen, as they are directly affected. It is reported that veterans have agreed to accept reduced pensions. However, the attitude of both veterans and civil servants will be revealed at a meeting scheduled for July 19th. Today, Laval delivered a radio address, urging the entire nation to cooperate in defending the stability of the franc, so that he can focus on dealing with diplomacy and handling peace affairs. (Reuters, 17th)

(Paris) After the government issued legal orders to balance the budget and reduce government spending, the trade unions of various public utilities decided to notify their members to hold demonstrations in Paris and the provinces to show their opposition. The various unions here have decided that, regardless of the circumstances, they will convene a large demonstration at the square in front of the National Theatre from 6:30 PM to 8:00 PM on Friday to protest the government's measures to reduce salaries. The Railway Workers' Union, the Postal Workers' Union, and the Unified General Confederation of Labour have joined forces. They believe that the government's mandated salary cuts for civil servants will have a far greater [unclear, illegible character] impact on middle and lower-level personnel than on senior personnel. As for the measures to reduce the cost of living stipulated in the order, they are, in practice, almost entirely superficial. Even if the cost of living is reduced, the proportion will certainly not match the proportion of salary reductions. (Havas, 17th)

(Paris) Twenty-four hours have passed since Laval's twenty-eight emergency decrees were issued. Criticism from the general public and commentary from newspapers is gradually increasing. Initially, the general opinion was that the government's measures were courageous, decisive, and admirable. Later, there was a feeling that the government's cuts to civil servants' salaries and other benefits had exceeded public expectations. Moreover, there was a major question as to whether living expenses could be reduced at the same time after the income of these people was reduced. The Socialist Party and its Communist Party newspapers unanimously attacked these decrees, advocating that all officials and civil servants rise up in [unclear, illegible character] opposition. The Railway Workers' Union and the Civil Servants' Union are now united in their opposition and have scheduled a meeting in front of a theater tomorrow to discuss how to respond, disregarding the government's ban on all outdoor gatherings. The National Assembly is also deeply dissatisfied. The Echo de Paris commented that these measures are overly sacrificial and feared that every French person would be affected. Furthermore, if the government's attempt to revive the economy fails again, it will plunge France into bankruptcy. Le Journal stated that these decrees are a decisive action by the government to restore its economic position. Le Petit Parisien stated that Laval will certainly use his extraordinary skills, wisdom, and confidence to promote the implementation of these decrees, and July 16th can be regarded as a major turning point for France to maintain its currency and revive the economy. (National Telegram, 18th)

(Paris) The cabinet meeting last night resolved to ban all demonstrations and marches so that the government could calmly implement its plans to protect the franc and implement austerity measures. The Ministry of the Interior warned the heads of all police stations to strictly comply with this order, which also prohibits gatherings of veterans and civil servants. (National Telegram, 18th)

(Paris) Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval delivered a radio address at 8:00 PM this evening, explaining the significance and scope of the government's distribution of substitute legal orders, stating that the main purpose of these measures is to maintain the value of the franc. He said, "Recently, regarding monetary policy, some people advocate devaluation, while others advocate inflating the currency. Those who advocate devaluation forget that the franc has already been devalued by four-fifths compared to the pre-war gold franc, while those who advocate currency inflation cannot avoid causing chaos in the monetary system. We cannot condone all of this and are willing to take a different path. The people celebrated the Republic Day and our free system last Sunday in a cheerful and solemn atmosphere. We must know that the Republic and freedom are difficult to preserve if the nation's finances cannot be independent, because there is no free country without sound finances." Laval also said that France's total national debt was 260,000,000,000 francs five years ago, but has now increased to 340,000,000,000 francs. (Havas, 17th)

(Paris) Prime Minister Laval made a five-minute radio broadcast address today, vehemently defending the emergency decrees issued yesterday to balance the budget and maintain the currency. Laval believed that France today only has two paths to take: one is a government with courage and action, and the other is revolution. The steps taken by the government today belong to the former. The government's actions are necessary to maintain the soundness of the French currency. The treasury must have a surplus to balance the budget, and if the budget cannot be balanced, political unrest will cause France to lose its prestige on the international stage. Although Laval's words were like this, the general public is extremely dissatisfied with the government's economic decrees. Former Minister of Subsidies, Rifflard, asked veterans to rise up in opposition, and the trade unions have also protested against the reduction of civil servants' salaries. (National Telegram, 18th)

(Paris) The emergency substitute legal order issued yesterday affects income from all aspects, so it is not welcomed, but it has not caused excessive resentment. The people of the whole country are dealing with it calmly. This order is actually gradually being recognized as necessary to reform the national finances and revive the industry. The reaction of the Paris Chamber of Commerce is quite good. Prime Minister Laval made a radio address to the nation tonight, saying that he would fully implement the austerity plan, and at the same time, he would take strong steps to restore industries. The French government must choose between devaluing the franc and protecting the franc. The people of the whole country will inevitably feel the same sacrifices, but after the economic situation improves, this sacrifice can be automatically reduced. (National Telegram, 17th)

Archduke Otto: Another Saying About Going to Austria

Brussels: It was learned here today that Archduke Otto of Habsburg, the successor to the Habsburg imperial family, is now planning to return to Austria to assume the position of regent without immediately taking the throne, and his mother, Empress Zita, will hold the title of regent. According to this plan, it was learned from a letter from Archduke Otto to the mayor of Langenlois, Austria, in which the Archduke thanked the mayor for inviting him to be an honorary citizen. (National Telegram, 17th)

(Vienna) Archduke Otto of Austria recently wrote to the mayor of Langenlois, roughly saying that he would come to Austria in the near future to take on the position of regent. However, this letter has been banned from publication by the government authorities today. According to speculation here, the possibility of Archduke Otto taking on the position of [unclear, illegible character] regent is very small. First, after this matter is realized, international disputes will immediately become more serious. Second, Prince Starhemberg is now seeking to monopolize power and may not be able to easily allow Otto to obtain this title. (National Telegram, 18th)

Bulgaria: Former Prime Minister Arrested; Said to Be Plotting a Coup

Vienna: According to unverified private news from the Bulgarian capital, the Bulgarian government has arrested former Prime Minister Georgiev to prevent a rumored coup against King Boris. (National Telegram, 17th)

Third International to Hold Congress

(Moscow) The Seventh Congress of the Communist International (i.e., the Third International) is about to open, and representatives from 59 countries will attend, with a total number of more than 400 people. Most of the representatives have already arrived here, but the locations where the prominent representatives are staying are kept secret, as the representatives are trying to avoid contact with people outside the Communist Party. Dimitrov, a Bulgarian Communist Party member who was detained on suspicion of arson in the German Reichstag fire case and released in February last year, will also attend this congress. It is generally believed that Dimitrov will be the most important figure in the Seventh Congress. He was originally from Bulgaria, but after coming to Russia, he acquired Soviet citizenship. His position in the Third International is becoming increasingly solid. Many members of the Communist Party believe that he is a promising figure in the future. Therefore, in this congress, he is likely to be elected chairman of the Third International after [Grigory] Zinoviev. (Note: Zinoviev was expelled from the Soviet Russian Communist Party in 1925 and removed from the position of chairman of the Third International.) Also, the Seventh Congress is expected to last for several weeks. The reports submitted by the representatives of the Communist Parties of various countries will be discussed separately. (Havas, 17th)

New French Cruiser Launched

Saint-Nazaire, France: The new cruiser "La Marseillaise" was launched here today. Navy Minister Pietri delivered a speech, saying that the government has decided to build six light cruisers for reconnaissance purposes. "La Marseillaise" is the second of these six ships. He also said that in the past 14 years, the total tonnage of ships built by public and private shipyards has reached 400,000 tons. The characteristic is that the ships built all belong to the same structural system and are no different. US Neutrality Bill

(Washington) There are three draft laws on the issue of neutrality. The first advocates prohibiting the transportation of arms to belligerent countries, and abolishing protection for domestic ships carrying goods to belligerent countries. The second advocates refusing to issue secret photos to US citizens traveling to belligerent countries. The third advocates prohibiting loans to belligerent countries. When the Senate Foreign Relations Committee discussed this issue today, Republican Senators Vandenberg and La Follette made passionate arguments, saying that Congress should promptly vote to abolish the protection of ships carrying goods to belligerent countries. The committee decided to form a subcommittee and order it to consult with experts from the State Department to agree on a satisfactory method so that the United States could maintain its neutrality in wartime. According to Secretary of State Hull, he had requested the Senate Foreign Relations Committee to postpone submitting to the Senate the two bills prohibiting loans to belligerent countries and refusing to issue passports to US citizens traveling to belligerent countries. At the committee meeting today, Republican Senator Nye, Democratic Senator Clark, and La Follette put forward arguments, saying that if the subcommittee cannot find a compromise solution, this issue should be directly submitted to the Senate for discussion by them. There are currently three trends regarding this issue in various aspects of the United States, and where to go is still undecided, namely: (1) The Senate favors the United States maintaining a neutral position, regardless of right or wrong; (2) The State Department wants to retain the right to determine which is the aggressor so that it can be blocked off alone; (3) The White House does not want Congress to pass any laws so that it can be used freely. The Foreign Affairs Committees of both houses of Congress are currently discussing the control bill for the manufacture and sale of arms. President Roosevelt hopes that after this bill is passed, it will satisfy all those who advocate neutrality and leave the Neutrality Bill to be discussed at the next session of Congress. This seems to be the continued effort of the senators so that they can achieve something. (Havas, 17th)

Wuhan New Flood Control Plan: Two Lines of Defense Constructed in Case of Emergency, Ye Peng Resigns, Chamber of Commerce Cables Requesting Retention, Liu Shoupeng Fully Responsible for Flood Control in the Provincial Capital

Hankou Communication: Since the day before yesterday, the river water has been receding. For the past two days, it has continued to recede by two inches. Today's water mark is 50 feet and one inch, and the situation is relatively relieved. However, the dikes are still not safe. Wuhan has formulated new flood control plans, and the responsible personnel have also changed. Initially, the entire Zhang Gong Dike in Hankou was in danger, and various sections presented dangerous signs from time to time. The Jianghan Engineering Bureau could not supply the necessary materials and was unable to carry out repairs on the spot, resulting in continued seepage and then collapse. The Gousao Tree section in the middle collapsed 30 to 40 yards in two days, and there was a risk of breach. Fortunately, all sectors of the Party, government, military, and police were fully mobilized, supervising and forcing more than 20,000 conscripted laborers to rescue desperately, averting the danger. Ye Peng, the director of flood control, and Wu Guozhen, the mayor who assisted in flood control, and Chen Xizeng, the director of public security, stayed on the dike, forgetting to eat and sleep for three days, and the tense atmosphere was evident. Today, the Gousao Tree dam construction project was completed. Ye resigned from his position as director due to illness. He Chengjun and Zhang Qun personally went to the Zhang Dike to persuade him to stay. Ye said that his hemorrhoids were very serious and that all the dangerous works had been repaired. He still handed over the flood control affairs of the dike to the Jianghan Engineering Bureau for full management. Wu Guozhen and Chen Xizeng also left the dike one after another, because yesterday's official and commercial meeting decided on a new flood control plan to raise the Pinghan Railway dike surface from Qiaokou to Nieko as the second line of defense. Wu and Chen both had to preside over this, so they really had no time to take care of the Zhang Dike. Today, the reporter visited Wu at Gousao Tree. According to him, the second line of defense was originally scheduled to start construction today, and 3,000 workers have been recruited, and 300,000 sandbags have also been ordered. Because other materials are not ready, the construction will be changed to tomorrow or the day after tomorrow. That evening, dangerous signs occurred again above and below Jingkou on the Zhang Dike. The Hankou Chamber of Commerce and the Hubei Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation held an emergency meeting to decide to cable Chairman Jiang, Director Zhang Xueliang, Chairman Zhang Qun, and Director He Chengjun to retain Ye Peng to continue to be responsible. The original telegram roughly stated, "This flood is rampant, continuing to rise, the Jianghan River is turbulent and the situation is dangerous, and the Zhang Gong Dike, which is relied upon as a guarantee for Hankou, is difficult to defend against, with continuous seepage and day and night repairs, with problems all around. It is feared that the situation from twenty years ago will be repeated. Since Commander Ye Peng was appointed as the director of flood control, he has rectified the work, unified the command, and worked on the dike for several consecutive days, not shirking his responsibility. Especially in the Gousao Tree section, the dike body collapsed and was in imminent danger. Thanks to Commander Ye's effective supervision of the construction and protection, the situation has now been turned from danger to safety. It was touch and go. Upon hearing that Commander Ye resigned due to illness, we were extremely shocked. We fear that a slight neglect in flood control will result in failure. We earnestly request your swift retention, so that he can immediately continue to be responsible and achieve complete success." In Wuchang, the construction of the second line of defense has now begun, starting from Hanyangmen and ending at Lufangkou. Because transportation of soil is more convenient, it can be completed within days. The original flood control committee had inconsistent authority. Today's plenary committee meeting decided to change the organization and appointed Director of the Construction Department Liu Shoupeng as the chairman, taking full responsibility for unified command, and Public Security Director Cai Mengjian and County Magistrate Yang Disheng as deputy directors. Yang was also ordered by the military camp to fully command the rescue work on the Wuzhong Dike, and another battalion of soldiers was dispatched to assist. If the water does not rise again, there may be no cause for concern. (17th)

Fujian Province Military Progress in Suppressing Bandits, Zhang, Zhou, Liu, and Su's Remaining Forces Now Being Encircled and Suppressed by Various Armies

Fuzhou Communication: After the division of districts and pacification in Fujian Province, the southern and northern Fujian areas have gradually been cleared of bandits. However, in Yongding and Pinghe counties in western Fujian, and in Dabu and Raoping areas bordering Guangdong, there are two groups led by Zhang Dingcheng and Zhou Lixing, who are harassing. They have been encircled and suppressed by the Fujian Army's Li Mo'an Division and the Guangdong Army's Huang Renhuan Division, but the bandits are able to break through and flee, making it difficult to wipe them out. After consultations between the armies of the two provinces, it was learned that the bandits were able to survive because they were familiar with the terrain, used remote villages and deep mountain valleys as nests, and used various means to oppress or lure villagers to be used by them and to provide them with food. Therefore, it was decided to implement a policy of clearing the fields and fortifying the walls, ordering the scattered people living in remote mountain villages to move within the defense lines of the stationed troops, taking out all food and utensils, and demolishing the houses so that the bandits could not gain a foothold on the plains. They can only flee into the mountains, and then the army will block the roads in and out of the mountains, so that they are surrounded in the mountains and cannot sneak into the villages to loot. Then, patrol teams will be organized to investigate and arrest scattered bandits in the border areas of the two provinces, in order to eliminate them as soon as possible. As for the Liu Ying and Su Yu groups in the eastern Fujian area, in the areas bordering Fuding, Shouning, and the Zhejiang Province counties of Taishun and Qingyuan, they once sneaked into the Zhejiang border, but were intercepted by the Zhejiang Security Team and retreated into Fujian territory. Colluding with local Communists Xie Zuolin, Fan Yisheng, and others, they are active in the three counties of Shouning, Xiapu, and Fu'an. Now, the 87th Division and the newly编 Tenth Division of the Security Regiment have each dispatched a part of their troops to advance towards the bandit areas. Yesterday, the Security Regiment defeated the Fan Yisheng group at Xietan, more than 30 li away from Shouning, killing four bandits and capturing seven alive. The remaining bandits fled towards the back mountain, and the regiment is pursuing them. Also, Liu brigade of the 87th Division also made contact with the Xie Zuolin group in the Tuoxi area of Xiapu County. Liu brigade selected soldiers to organize a lightly armed guerrilla team, with 20 to 30 people in a group, to go deep into the bandit area to search and clear the ambush. Furthermore, the First Regiment of the New Tenth Division encountered a pseudo-guerrilla team in Guanyang, Fu'an, the day before yesterday, and a fierce battle broke out. They held each other for a day and a night, but the bandits did not retreat. Afterwards, the government troops launched a forward charge, and the bandits could not hold on and began to flee towards Shangqi. Guanyang was then recovered by the government troops. Yesterday, the New Tenth Division dispatched personnel to escort more than 200 rifles, several mortars, and other trophies seized in the bandit suppression operations in eastern Fujian to the province for delivery to the Ordnance Department for storage. (July 17)

A Lubricating Old Man Accuses Ma Zhanshan of Forcibly Claiming to Be His Son, Who Had Escaped Out as a Child, After Investigation, the False Accusation Is Reversed

Tianjin Communication: Ma Zhanshan has been living in seclusion in the British Concession of Tianjin for a long time. Unexpectedly, a few days ago, he was suddenly accused by an old man from Fengrun County, Ma Rong, who claimed that Ma Zhanshan was his own son, who had left home as a child. Now that he had found his whereabouts, he went to seek recognition, but was rejected. Therefore, he had no choice but to accuse him of abandoning his parents. After the District Prosecutor's Office approved the complaint, it immediately summoned both parties to court for investigation at 10:00 a.m. on the 12th of this month. The plaintiff, Ma Rong, reported his arrival, wearing a blue gauze mandarin jacket, a blue feather gauze gown, blue silk socks, blue formal wool shoes, and an old-fashioned straw hat. Although he was over seventy years old, he was still in good spirits. On that day, Ma Zhanshan sent his secretary, Du Gouruo, to report on his behalf. At about 11:00 a.m., the prosecutor, Yu Jiancheng, opened the court and interrogated them separately. He questioned the plaintiff in great detail and briefly questioned the defendant's representative. He ordered the court to be opened at 10:00 a.m. on the 13th, and Ma Zhanshan himself had to appear in court.

Ma Zhanshan's Statement

According to Ma Zhanshan, "My ancestral home is indeed Fengrun County, but I have been living in Huaide County, Liaoning, for about ten generations. My father's name was Ma Chun. He had three brothers, ranking third. My eldest uncle, Ma Guang, and my second uncle, Ma Ling, are both deceased. Now I have several nephews who are all in Tianjin. My father died of illness in Huaide on September 26th of the sixth year of the Republic of China, at the age of 57. At that time, I was serving as a battalion commander. When he was buried, all relatives and friends were notified, and everyone knew about it. My mother, Liu, died of illness when I was eleven years old. I was taught by my father most of the time. This spring, Ma Rong, an old man, asked to see me. I met him twice in the courtyard. He said that I was his son and that I had a hitching post behind my left ear. I asked him to touch it, but there was no such characteristic. He said that I was not the real Ma Zhanshan and must be an impostor. I thought that he might have lost a son and was sick with worry, so I did not want to investigate further. I asked people to persuade him to leave. Unexpectedly, he actually filed a complaint in court. According to him, I am 52 years old and was born on the eighth day of the twelfth lunar month, which is completely wrong. I am now 51 years old and was born on October 25th at midnight. The accusations are obviously absurd. Because I have special circumstances, it is inconvenient for me to appear in court to confront him, but if necessary, I will definitely appear in court in person."

Ma Rong's Statement

According to Ma Rong, "I am currently 73 years old, a native of Fengrun County, east of Tianjin, living in Zhongxin Village. I have two sons and one daughter. The eldest son, named Zhanshan, was born to my ex-wife, Lü. The second son was born to my second wife in Qianjinzai, outside the pass, and is named Shoushan. He is currently 33 years old and still outside the pass. Zhanshan's childhood name was Laohu. He was born on the eighth day of the twelfth lunar month in the tenth year of the reign of Emperor Guangxu of the Qing Dynasty. After he was born, I went to Qianjinzai to work as a cook in a shop and did not often go home. When Zhanshan was seven years old, in the sixteenth year of the reign of Emperor Guangxu, his mother, Lü, died of illness. He then begged for a living with his "two braids," begging during the day and sleeping on the streets at night, which was very pitiful. Later, I returned to Fengrun and managed to send the two children to a friend's house for foster care. I still went out to earn a living. When Zhanshan was twelve years old, his sister died of illness, and Zhanshan also disappeared. After inquiring everywhere, there was no news. I returned to Qianjinzai and remarried. After the September 18th Incident, I heard about the anti-Japanese hero Ma Zhanshan, and I suspected that he was my lost son, but I had no way to prove it. Later, a fellow villager, Bai, who was a train driver, said that he had seen Ma Zhanyou and that he was indeed my lost son. I then had the intention to find him, but I could not pass through because of the chaos. Later, I heard that his troops had arrived in Harbin. I went there alone, but there was a flood in that place, and I did not succeed. On October 26th of last year, I went to Beiping to inquire, but he was not in Beiping. I returned to Tangyou to my relatives and entrusted Ma Fa of Xiaomazhuang, Fengrun County, to inquire. Because Ma was the father-in-law of the former Tianjin Mayor Zhang Ting'e, I was helped by him and received a letter from Mayor Zhang. Later, I received a reply saying that Ma Zhanshan was indeed a native of Fengrun County and now lives in the British Concession of Tianjin. Because I had lost my son for forty years, I was very happy to have found his whereabouts. So I came to Tianjin on the eighth day of the first lunar month this year. I went to the British Concession to find him, but his servants would not allow us father and son to meet. Unable to do so, I went back again and entrusted Ma Fa to write a letter, writing in detail my photo and the childhood of Zhanshan. Later, Ma Zhanshan replied, still not admitting it, saying that I was talking nonsense. So I came to find him many times again, but still could not see him. Once, he sent a person surnamed Fu to see me, and I scolded him. The last time, I saw him inside the door, but he still would not recognize me, so I filed a complaint."

False Accusation Is Reversed

At about 11:00 a.m. on the 13th, the court was reopened for investigation. Ma Zhanshan did not appear in court and sent his secretary, Du Gouruo, again, bringing with him an enlarged full-body photo of Ma Zhanshan himself. Regarding the two points of Ma Rong's accusation, (1) the son that Ma Rong recognized as lost had a hitching post next to his ear, but Ma Zhanshan did not. (2) The son that Ma Rong lost was 52 years old and was born on the eighth day of the twelfth lunar month, while Ma Zhanshan himself was 51 years old and was born on October 24th. In addition, Ma Zhanshan lived in Huaide for ten generations, and everyone knew about it. There were relatives and friends who could testify. Moreover, the son that Ma Rong lost was originally named Jinshan, while Ma Zhanshan was originally named Zhenbang. When he reached the position of battalion commander, Wu Junsheng changed his name to Zhanshan on his behalf. He refuted them one by one. Ma Rong still said that the photo was a forgery and that Ma Zhanshan himself had to appear in court or list three generations of ancestors. The court believed that Ma Rong's reasons were insufficient and dismissed him immediately, allowing for further investigation next time. At the same time, Du Gouruo, representing Ma Zhanshan, filed a charge of false accusation against Ma Rong, using the above points as reasons to prove that Ma Rong fabricated facts and insulted his reputation. The Prosecutor's Office immediately accepted the case, interrogated him, and ordered Ma Rong to post bail and await summons. This matter has proven that although Ma Rong did lose a son, it was not the Ma Zhanshan he was referring to. He only had this recognition because he missed his son so much. It is said that when Ma Rong went to Ma's residence several times before, Ma Zhanshan thought that he was old and missed his son, which was understandable, and intended to help him so that he could go to find him. Unexpectedly, Ma Rong believed that this Ma was that Ma and ended up filing a complaint. As a result, the evidence was not accurate, which can be said to be superfluous. (13th)

Guangdong Holds Police Guard Conference

—Proposals Focus on Training and Funding—

Guangzhou Communication: Since Guangdong Province has organized police guard teams in various counties, districts, and villages, the reserve and preparatory teams of various counties have been trained one after another, and the local self-defense forces have gradually established a foundation. However, in terms of funding, the fees have been taken from the field donation. Recently, the financial authorities changed the land tax levy and cancelled the food money. The local police guard funding association should also be abolished at the same time. In the future, police fees will be paid by the county government from the land tax retention counties. In order to coordinate the police guard affairs of the entire province, the authorities have scheduled a provincial police guard conference on the 8th of this month. Prior to that, each pacification area was ordered to first convene the deputy directors of the compilation and training offices of each county in the pacification area to hold a police guard preparatory meeting in each district office in order to collect proposals and submit them to the conference for discussion. Until the end of last month, the police guard preliminary meetings in each pacification area were held in turn. The provincial police guard conference was held as scheduled on the 8th of this month. The meeting place was in the guard office of the headquarters on Yuehua Road. The attendees included Luo Xianxiang, director of the military affairs department of the East District Pacification Office, Wang Hongrao, director of the military affairs department of the South District Pacification Office, Liu Zhenyuan, director of the military affairs department of the Northwest District Pacification Office, Liu Shiliang, director of the military affairs department of the Qiongyai Pacification Office, Liu Weishan, director of the military affairs department of the Central District Pacification Office, and Feng Zhuoxun, director of the guard office of the headquarters, police guard inspectors Xue Hanguang, Chen Jing, Geng Hanchi, Liang Fangpu, etc. The opening ceremony was held at 8:00 a.m. that morning. Chairman Chen Jitang gave a speech to the officers, with the main idea of ​​encouraging the officers in charge to earnestly train the police guard teams, create a strong popular armed force, defend the local area, directly defend themselves and indirectly defend the country. Chen left his seat after speaking, and then Chairman Feng Zhuoxun reported on the meeting matters. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 noon. In the afternoon, a meeting was held to sort out the proposals. The meeting continued on the 9th to discuss the proposals. It was heard that there were more than 100 proposals from various districts. Those with the same nature were merged separately, for a total of more than 80 cases. The cases were mostly about reforms in training and issues of income and expenditure. The meeting will not be adjourned until all cases have been discussed.

Qin Dechun Delays Return to Zhangyuan Due to Illness, Song Zheyuan's Whereabouts Still Undetermined, Xiao Zhenying Returns to Beiping to Comfort Qin on Behalf of Song

Beiping Communication: Regarding the position of Chairman of the Chahar Provincial Government, since Song Zheyuan was dismissed and the Central Government ordered Qin Dechun, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, to act as his agent, Qin initially sent a telegram expressing his desire to advance and retreat with Song due to moral considerations, leaving Zhang to come to Beiping. Later, due to a sense of responsibility, he was responsible in Beiping for handling the Zhangbei negotiations with the Japanese side. Afterwards, because Song's whereabouts have not yet been resolved, his desire to leave became stronger and his intentions became particularly negative. Chahar Provincial Committee member Xiao Zhenying had been running around to stabilize the Chahar situation as soon as possible, but the result was to wait for the central government's decision.

At the beginning of the Central Government's dismissal order, Song Zheyuan resolutely left Zhangyuan and returned to Tianjin to rest, taking care of the overall situation. Qin, who had followed Song for many years, although he received an explicit order to act as his agent, did not actually take office due to his private friendship. His continuation of handling the Zhangbei negotiations after requesting resignation was probably driven by a sense of responsibility to serve the country. During the negotiation period, Qin's hard work and willingness to bear hardships were known to everyone. Therefore, after the settlement of the negotiations, Qin planned to move to a quiet place to recuperate, both to treat his insomnia and to change the air.

Qin Dechun was originally scheduled to return to Zhangyuan within days to handle the affairs of the Civil Affairs Department. However, because there were matters to be negotiated with the Japanese side in handling the aftermath of the Zhangbei negotiations, the date of return to Zhang has not yet been determined. Matsui, the military liaison officer of the Kwantung Army stationed in Zhangyuan, came to Beiping yesterday (13th) morning and visited Qin with Takahashi Tan, the military attaché of the Japanese Embassy in Beiping, for a long talk. The content was nothing more than discussing the aftermath of eastern Chahar. According to unofficial sources that evening, at the end of the talks, Qin had been working hard for a long time and had collapsed once. He was revived with ginger soup.

So far today (13th), it has been proven that Qin suffered hemoptysis last night (12th), and the situation is serious. Many Chinese and Western doctors were urgently invited to diagnose and verify that the small blood vessels at the costal cartilage joint between the eighth and ninth ribs of Qin had ruptured, and it was not lung disease. Although there was no major danger, the doctor ordered absolute rest and no movement. Qin originally planned to be admitted to the hospital for treatment, but he had to stay at home to rest. Upon hearing of his illness, people came to visit and express their condolences, but Qin did not receive them.

Xiao Zhenying went to Tianjin on official business a few days ago and originally planned to stay for a short time. Upon receiving the news of Qin's illness, he returned to Beiping at 6:42 p.m. today (13th). According to him, Qin's illness was not a major problem, and he hoped that he would recover soon. His return to Beiping was purely to visit him. Song (Zheyuan) was very concerned about Qin's illness. His trip to Sichuan was temporarily postponed. After leaving the station, Xiao went to Fuyou Street to meet him and conveyed Song's intentions.

Reorganization and Establishment of the All-Zhejiang Native Place Association

The Ningbo and Shaoxing natives in Kunshan County originally had a native place association organization, with a history of over a hundred years. The association's assets were quite substantial. However, there were few members, so the association's affairs were handled by the chairman, Xu Jingbo. Approval was immediately obtained from the political authorities for preparation. By the 15th, everything was ready. Representatives from various agencies also attended the meeting. Over two hundred members were present. Li Zhihui served as chairman, performing the rituals. Li reported on the preparations. The association's constitution was then discussed, followed by the election of nine executive committee members: Li Zhihui, Chen Boying, Ma Huating, Chen Yuxian, Han Zhimin, Chen Yuyu, Xu Chufang, Guo Linshan, and Kuang Chunfan. Zhang Wenxin, Chen Zhiren, and Wang Jianbo were elected as alternate executive committee members. Yin Shenong, Xu Jingbo, and Luo Xingwei were elected as supervisory committee members. Fifty-Nine Straw Sheds Burned Down

The Niupengtou area outside the Tongyang Bridge South, outside the South Gate, is a gathering place for immigrants from north of the Yangtze River, with straw sheds lined up densely. At 4 p.m. the day before yesterday (the 17th), a fire broke out in the straw shed of A San's family, accidentally spreading to the neighboring sheds. The fire blazed into the sky, making it difficult to control. Fire brigades from various sections rushed to the scene to extinguish the fire, which was eventually put out. A total of fifty-nine sheds were burned down, with losses estimated at over ten thousand yuan. The cause of the fire was determined to be Liu's wife, who was cooking a fried egg dish and negligently left the fire near firewood.

Appeal to Exempt Cloth Factories from Double Taxation

The Cloth Factory Trade Association of this county stated that factories such as Meiheng, Daxin, Jinghua, Yunhua, Zhenye, and Xinyi are all located in the rural areas and have already paid business tax. In the urban areas, they only have transshipment locations. The import and export of yarn and cloth are not sales activities. Now, the Business Tax Bureau is ordering them to pay tax, which is not only double taxation but also increases the cost of national loans and hinders sales. This is contrary to the government's aim to promote industry. Yesterday, they sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, requesting that, according to the Business Tax Collection Regulations, the Department of Finance and the Department of Industry be instructed to order the bureau to stop this practice to protect domestic goods. They also requested that the Business Tax Bureau be informed in advance that direct collection from cloth factories should be suspended until instructions are received from the departments to avoid disputes.

Autumn Locusts Found Again in the Seventh District

Locust nymphs previously appeared in the reeds of Zhaiqiao, Fangqian Qianlingtai, and Dacheng and other four townships in the Seventh District of Wujin. However, the locusts were not caught in time in Yixing, so swarms of locusts occasionally flew over. The Department of Construction ordered that measures be taken to eliminate them. He then returned to the district. He Xiqi, the deputy director of the Sericulture Improvement District, inspected the actual situation on the afternoon of the 18th, in order to start eliminating them and avoid the spread of the harm.

Zhenjiang

Select High-Quality Seeds for Grain Storage

The Jiangsu Provincial Government considers warehouse storage an important administrative priority for famine relief. In recent years, various counties have suffered from frequent droughts and floods, and impoverished farmers have been unable to afford seeds. Although various counties have the practice of storing grain for seed, it has been stored for too long, and its germination ability is limited. In the future, when counties increase their grain reserves, 70% of the increase should be stored for famine relief, and 30% should be used to select high-quality seeds, distinguishing their types, and storing them in separate warehouses. The following points should be noted regarding the storage of high-quality seeds: (1) Seeds produced in the current year should be selected for purchase and storage; (2) Purchase should be made locally so that the seeds can adapt to the local climate and fully develop; (3) Seeds with higher yields should be selected, and those that are free from insect pests and diseases; (4) Attention should be paid to the ventilation and humidity control of the warehouse to prevent the stored grains from losing their ability to germinate; (5) Before storage, wind winnowing or screening should be used to eliminate inferior seeds and remove impurities; (6) If the seeds are distributed to farmers for use, the warehouse should guide the farmers in using saltwater to select seeds and immersing them in warm water. The parts regarding storing grain for famine relief should still follow the various regulations of the local warehouse storage management rules, the outline of the measures for storing grain for famine relief, and the detailed rules for the food management committee of each county, strictly managing the storage and paying close attention to the quality when purchasing and storing the grain. The provincial government ordered the Department of Construction to select and dispatch specialized personnel during the harvest period to investigate and designate the best seeds for purchase and storage. It also formulated a method for managing seeds and issued instructions to the county governments to comply with it.

Jiaxing

Resolution of Weicheng Silk Factory Dispute

All the male and female workers of the Jiaxing Weicheng Qingji Silk Factory appealed to the Party and government for relief because the factory had decided to increase working hours and reduce wages starting from the 8th. After many days of mediation by the Party and government authorities and Gu Suming, chairman of the county chamber of commerce, an agreement was finally reached because neither side was willing to yield. The workers resumed work on the 12th. It is understood that from then on, wages would be increased by four points per machine and per worker. The three-shift system was changed to a two-shift system, and wages were increased by five points. The tenth-day promotion was still given as before. Both sides have reached an understanding and the dispute has been resolved.

Correspondence

Letter from Lawyer Zhang Tianbai

To the editor: I am writing on behalf of my client, Pan Baorong, who claims that he was astonished to read a news item titled "Xiding Thoroughly Investigates Qingwen Zhang Wu's Embezzlement" in the local correspondence section of the Shen Bao on July 9th. After investigation, it was found that Zhang Baorong's position is as the drawing team leader and internal inspector. According to the inspection rules, he has the authority to correct errors in Wu's map. Zhang Baorong has corrected no less than thousands of Qingzhang maps in various villages in Jiading County, as evidenced by the land registration book. Moreover, there is no ownerless public land in Jiading Fifth District, except for Yangzhong, so Beixin Township, where Baorong resides, is part of the Fifth District and is naturally no exception. Furthermore, the land deeds purchased by Baorong have the signatures of the original owners and intermediaries, so how could they be forged? All of the Sichuan products owned by Baorong have been applied for registration, and the public announcement is about to expire. No affected owners have filed a complaint. This clearly shows that Baorong has not engaged in any embezzlement while serving in the Qingzhang team. Moreover, the Jiangsu Provincial Land Bureau has not sent anyone to Jiading to investigate this case recently. Ribao Rong has been sick and has requested to resign since July 1st, but has not yet received Tenfeng's approval after half a month. Therefore, the rumor of suspension is unfounded. It is evident that all the reported sections are untrue. Therefore, I am writing to the Shen Bao on behalf of my client to request an immediate correction. I hope that you will publish this letter in the "Correspondence" section. I am, [signed] Lawyer Zhang Tianbai, July 18th.

Local News

Opium Treatment Hospitals to be Established in Zhabei, Western Shanghai, Pudong, etc.; as Many Beds as Possible to be Provided for Forced Admission

According to Guomin She, since the establishment of the Anti-Opium Commission in Maojianong, Nanshi, this city, on the 1st of this month, the commission has been implementing measures for opium prohibition. Police Chief Cai Jingjun has instructed all bureaus and stations to assign personnel to register opium smokers within their jurisdictions. Health Bureau Chief Li Ting'an has ordered the vigorous expansion of opium treatment centers to accommodate as many opium smokers as possible for treatment. However, the existing Longhua Opium Treatment Center and the Nanshi Municipal Public Hospital are inadequate due to the limited number of beds. Therefore, opium treatment hospitals will be established in Zhabei, Western Shanghai, and Pudong within the shortest possible time. Plans call for the hospitals to provide as many beds as possible to force opium smokers to enter for treatment. It is said that the establishment of these opium treatment hospitals is currently in the fundraising stage and will be implemented soon.

The National Goods Alliance Suggests Controlling Industry; will Submit Detailed Plans to the Ministry for Approval and Request Expedited Loans from the Ministry of Finance

The National Goods Promotion Alliance Committee of this city held a standing committee meeting at its headquarters at 3 p.m. yesterday. More than ten people attended, including Gu Xiyuan, Hu Xiyuan, Lu Guozhuang, Zhang Zilian, Jiang Zhonghe, Ma Jisheng, Cheng Shouchong, Wang Xingyi, Chen Yiting, and Lu Zhixue. The meeting was chaired by Lu Zhixue. It was reported that in recent years, various light industries in our country have seemed to progress rapidly on the surface, but in reality, the unrestricted establishment of factories and the production of shoddy goods have caused the credit of domestic goods to decline sharply. Industrial products cannot reach perfection without sophisticated equipment and years of experimentation and research. However, it often happens that foremen or assistants of factories, who know only a little, go out and set up factories. With extremely simple equipment and extremely loose organization, they launch products on the market in just a few months, and even claim to be old brands. This is truly absurd. The inferiority of their products is imaginable, so they can only use low prices to attract customers. Society is dissatisfied with them, and this leads to a general loss of faith in domestic goods. People would rather buy foreign goods. This has a huge impact on domestic factories that produce high-quality products, and the crime of inducing Chinese people to send their money abroad is even greater. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's request that the government implement industrial control is based on this reason. Some believe that after the implementation of industrial control, the number of factories will inevitably decrease, making the unemployment problem even more serious. However, factories that produce substandard products cannot stabilize themselves, and factories that produce standard products cannot consolidate themselves due to the price disruption. Perhaps they will all perish together, making the unemployment problem even more serious. However, the workers of factories with high-quality products and more developed businesses will naturally increase, which is better than the former situation. As a large group of domestic factories, the alliance should submit a presentation stating the urgency and necessity of industrial control while the government is still hesitant about the industrial control issue, and request that it be put on the agenda for implementation as soon as possible. As for the detailed rules for industrial control, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has already drafted them in detail and submitted them to the government. The alliance should have its own proposals, and at the same time report the progress of the loan application. As a result of the discussion, (1) It was resolved to submit a request to the Ministry of Finance for a quick loan to industrial and commercial businesses to save them from their plight. (2) It was resolved that the entire plan for industrial control should be reported to the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry should adopt and approve it in accordance with the Ministry of Industry's approval.

China Will Send a Delegation to Thailand to Investigate; The Delegation is Expected to Consist of Nine People Organized by Business Circles of this City

Since the Thai government's mistreatment of Chinese expatriates has caused indignation among Chinese people and triggered a boycott of Thai rice, its merchants have been significantly affected. Our country also intends to send a delegation, expected to consist of nine people, organized by the business circles of this city, including six representatives of organizations and three leaders of industry and commerce. Its main task is to investigate the businesses of overseas Chinese and the industrial and commercial conditions in Thailand.

After staying in Shanghai for a short time, he will return to Beijing to complete the transfer of the Supreme Court.

Requests for Disaster Relief for Flood-Stricken Provinces

Communications Received from the Red Swastika Society

Since the beginning of summer, mountain floods have erupted in various places. Hubei, Jiangxi, and other provinces have already suffered disasters in succession. The counties of Fancheng, Tianmen, and Gucheng are especially devastated. In recent days, the Yellow River has also breached its banks, and the provinces of Shandong and Hebei have suffered renewed catastrophes. The Joint Office of the Southeast Branches of the Red Swastika Society in this city has successively received requests for disaster relief from the Red Swastika Societies in Hubei, Shandong, and other provinces. These are recorded below. (1) Telegram from the Jiangxi Provincial Disaster Relief Committee: Raise funds for the drought relief associations of various provinces. Red Swastika Society General Office. Hua Yang Righteous Disaster Relief General Association, please note. En Wei two telegrams, all seen and considered. Jiangxi Province has suffered both banditry and frequent droughts and floods. Without urgent relief, the lives of the people will be difficult to sustain. In addition to the previous report to your association of 13 counties affected by floods, for a total of 24 counties in three reports, we now additionally report Wuyuan, Leping, Fengxin, Dongxiang, Pengze, Yiyang, Yujiang, Duchang, Guangfeng, Guixi, Qianshan, and other twelve counties reporting flood disasters. The situation is especially severe. It is observed that this major flood is causing disasters, and the rising water exceeds all previous records. In some places, the water level has risen by more than 18 feet in a single night. Currently, the Yangtze River and Poyang Lake are both experiencing floods, advancing simultaneously. The inland areas are flooded, and there is no way to drain the water. Many embankments have been submerged and breached. Even those that have survived are in constant fear. The displaced people have left their homes and live in the mountains, lacking food. Cries for help shake the mountains, and telegrams of urgency are like stars in the sky. If urgent relief is not provided, they may resort to desperate measures, which is a cause for concern. This committee lacks the resources to provide aid and has no magic touch. We cannot bear to ignore their plight, but we are also unable to help with our bare hands. In this time of dire need, we can only send another telegram to plead for the people's lives. We humbly request that you consider the extraordinary severity of the disaster in Jiangxi and immediately provide charitable assistance to save the lives of the people. The entire population is eagerly awaiting your benevolent response. Jiangxi Provincial Disaster Relief Committee Chairman Lu Xianjia (seal). (1) Telegram from the Wuhan Office: The embankments in the various counties of Hubei have been breached one after another, causing losses to crops and drowning people. The severity of the disaster and the extent of the affected area are even greater than in the year of Xinwei [1931]. More than 30 large ships have been dispatched to Hankou to handle emergency relief nearby. We earnestly request that you quickly raise funds for assistance. We respectfully plead for the lives of the people in more than 20 counties. (1) Telegram from the Yichang Red Swastika Society: Yichang has been experiencing continuous rain for four days and nights. Floods converge, and the water depth in the plains is more than ten feet. Crops and houses have been swept away by the flood. Countless people and livestock have died. The situation is extremely tragic. We have organized rescue teams together with people from all walks of life to provide rescue and relief. What is especially tragic is that in the Xiaoxita area, more than 400 households were washed away by the water in one night, leaving only about 20 households. More than 500 people died. In total, more than 20,000 people in this city have been affected by the disaster, without clothing or food. We urgently request that funds be allocated for relief. (1) Telegram from the Jiujiang Red Swastika Society: The Yangtze River is overflowing. The counties of Tianmen and Gucheng in Hubei Province have been completely submerged. The bodies of people and livestock are floating down the river past Xun. Our society has formed teams to retrieve and bury the bodies. Please inform the branches in Qing, Tong, Wu, and Jing to pay attention in their respective areas to prevent epidemics. Jiujiang Branch, Qia. (1) Telegram from Fancheng: On the night of July 6th, Fancheng experienced torrential rain. By the morning of the 7th, the Xiang River had risen violently by more than ten feet. The houses in the city were submerged, and even the higher places were blocked by the flood. Thousands of people were drowned, and half of the houses collapsed. Outside the city, there was a vast expanse of water, and the number of dead was even greater. The heartbreaking and tragic scene cannot be described by any words in the dictionary. By the morning of the 10th, the water level had receded slightly, and the city was filled with cries of mourning, even more tragic than before. The dead cannot be buried, and the living, whether rich or poor, are all crying out for food. Local government agencies and gentry have formed a flood relief committee to provide temporary relief to the victims. However, the flood was so fierce that the water rose by more than six feet in an hour, making it impossible to escape in time. Goods and food were all submerged by the water. This is an unprecedented catastrophe. The victims are on the verge of death, desperately hoping for relief. In addition, Fancheng's commerce has collapsed in recent years and is no longer a city. How can they survive this great hardship? We urgently report the situation and earnestly plead for immediate relief to save the lives of the people. Your great kindness and virtue will be forever remembered. Fancheng City Flood Relief Committee (seal). (1) Telegram from the Jinan Red Swastika Society: The Zhencheng River has breached its banks, and the water is flowing southeast, causing severe disasters in Heze, Yuncheng, Juye, Dongping, Jiaxiang, and other counties. The flood season is still ongoing, and it is difficult to block the breach. The Jinan Society has sent a rescue team to Zhencheng to handle emergency relief. However, the disaster is widespread, and funds are lacking. We deeply hope that all branches will quickly raise funds and send personnel to provide emergency relief. Jinan Swastika Society, Pu.

It is reported that after receiving the telegrams, the organization sent the tragic details of the floods in Hubei and Shandong to various branches in the southeast, calling for a joint effort to raise funds for relief. Telegrams were also sent to the branches in Jing, Wu, Tong, and Qing to quickly form rescue teams to retrieve and bury floating corpses along the river to prevent epidemics.
