Metals: Ribbed Steel Bars Difficult to Recover - Impact of Declining Construction Industry

40-foot-long ribbed steel bars are essential for the construction industry. However, with frequent declines in land prices in Shanghai, construction projects have been greatly reduced. Furthermore, foreign traders are facing rural collapse, economic panic, and widespread flooding, which has greatly reduced the demand for this type of construction material. Frequent arrivals have resulted in huge stockpiles. Due to economic conditions, some traders are willing to sell at low prices, but there are few buyers. The standard is negatively affected by the adverse environment, leading to a worsening situation. Quotations for mixed colors are 90 yuan per ton. Retail prices range from 105 yuan to 87 yuan. In the past three days, only 40-50 tons have been offered for sale on the market, a decrease of one-third compared to the prosperous period. Therefore, it is feared that it will not be easy for the market to recover in the short term.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Zhu Weixuan)

The closing-down sale of small shops has almost become a new advertising technique in 1939, because although they shout closing down every day, they rarely actually do so. On the contrary, large companies and banks that boast about their strong capital and prosperous business often collapse with the speed of lightning and without any prior warning. This is probably the difference between large companies and small shops?

As the saying goes: "The benevolent see benevolence, and the wise see wisdom"! This describes how each person sees things differently, so one should not criticize others' good and bad based on personal subjective opinions. Often, a profligate son who gambles and indulges in pleasure until he is ruined is considered a bad person by everyone, but he is often considered a good person in brothels and gambling dens!

Why Walk on the Left?

— Pei Yu

I remember that one of the tenets of the New Life Movement was "Walk on the left." The purpose of establishing this tenet was probably to avoid congestion and maintain order. But why walk on the left and not on the right? If vehicles drive on the right and people also walk on the right, wouldn't it achieve the same effect of avoiding congestion and maintaining order? According to a British researcher, after much research, he has come up with a very reasonable and interesting explanation. He said that walking on the left is closely related to human physiology.

Here, let's first study a question, why are most of us better at using our right hand? It is said that because the heaviest organ in our body, the "liver", is located on the right side. Because the liver is on the right, we can easily turn from the right to the left. In this way, people in ancient times found that it was easier to wave a stick or throw a stone with their right hand than with their left hand. After many eras, the right hand continued to be easier to train than the left hand.

The use of hands is like this, but riding a horse is the opposite. Getting on the horse from the left side, which is opposite to the side where the liver is located, and staying close to the side of the road is safer. Therefore, the rule of walking on the left side of the road was passed down from the time when everyone rode horses. However, on British pavements, you have to walk on the right, because it is easier to get off the horse or vehicle on the right side of the pavement. The road rule "walk on the left" and the pavement rule "walk on the right" both came from the relationship between riding and physiology.

Wooden Fish and Dragon Boat Songs

— Lan Shan

I recently read Mr. Zhang Yide's "Wooden Fish" article in this journal, which introduced Cantonese folk literature to us, and I admire it very much. However, Mr. Zhang has misunderstood many places in the article, and there are also places that are not explained in detail. The following is a supplement and correction.

Mr. Zhang said that "Wooden Fish" is like a short essay, and "Bullet Songs" is like a long novel, which is wrong. In fact, "Wooden Fish" is a very lengthy segmented song, just like a novel. It takes more than a whole day to sing the whole book. However, something that resembles a short story or essay is another kind, not called "Wooden Fish", but the very famous "Dragon Boat Song".

Because "Wooden Fish" is too long, not everyone can sing it. But "Dragon Boat Songs" are short and concise, with melancholy and lingering emotions, and everyone remembers and likes to hum a few verses.

"Wooden Fish" such as "Purple Xia Cup", "Jade Sunflower Fan", "Unbinding the Red Silk Robe", "Liang Shanbo and Zhu Yingtai", etc. are really magnificent, with tens of thousands to hundreds of thousands of words. After the old lady finishes her supper, she is encouraged by her daughters-in-law and maids to put on her reading glasses and start singing. She can sing four or five sections in an hour.

The Dragon Boat Song is different, everyone can sing it. We who are called "A Shao" can sing it, and so can the maids and servants. The most common ones are "Autumn Regret on a Journey", "Chen Shimei Denies His Wife", "Bin Yu Cries at the Funeral" and "He Huiqun Sighs at the Fifth Watch".

"The silkworm spins silk until it dies, and the candle sheds tears until it is ash. A good marriage is achieved, but it fills me with endless sorrow. A spring dream is empty, all because of shallow fate and no cause for love..." These are wonderful lines from the funeral song. As for "Autumn Regret on a Journey" and "Sighing at the Fifth Watch", which are unanimously praised by the literati, they are both Dragon Boat Songs, with beautiful words and sad and poignant tones, which can be sung a hundred or a thousand times without getting tired.

Singing "Wooden Fish" and "Dragon Boat Songs" is not without rhythm and pitch, as Mr. Zhang said, but it must follow a certain tune, which we call "Southern Music", with ups and downs, which is very pleasant to the ear. In short, "Wooden Fish" and "Dragon Boat Songs" are mostly based on love between men and women. Although there are works that are loyal to the emperor and patriotic, they are not to people's liking, so they are shelved.

In Guangdong, there is a kind of "blind girl" who sells songs, singing a good "Dragon Boat Song" and "Wooden Fish" for a very low price.

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Sixteen: The Curtain Hides Tears Hard to Escape Cold Eyes, Clothing Brags About Luck, Meeting Power

He smiled and said: Mr. Cheng, there is one thing, quite sorry to you. Zhiqian smiled and said: What are you talking about? We are new friends to each other, and there is not much to it. Where does these three words "sorry" come from? Jie Fu smiled: I don't need to say this, I think you know. It's just... Saying, his voice lowered, and he laughed, "It's just that Miss Zhu has already been kept in a golden house by Brother Duocai." Originally, this child was very interested in you, but this is a bit of you letting go. Zhiqian was initially angry and his face turned purple. After a thought, he laughed, and smoothed the purple color on his face. Because said: These words can be said to be far away. Mr. Jia's concubine has nothing to do with me. Even if it interferes with me, you can't ask Mr. Zhang to apologize to me. Isn't this thing very interesting? Jie Fu said: No, I am very good with Mr. Jia, I can represent say sorry. Zhiqian thought for a while and laughed: Is this from Mr. Jia's meaning? Or is it from Mr. Zhang's meaning? Jie Fu said: Mr. Jia has an intention, but it is inconvenient for him to say it. I just came back from the two places of the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Construction, and I talked with Duocai for a long time. Zhiqian said: Is the bride very happy? Jie Fu said: That's natural. Don't you see me wearing a mandarin jacket? I am because of seeing the two directors. Otherwise; adding a mandarin jacket is also very hot. Zhiqian said: That girl has changed from being so poor that she wants to beg for food, to becoming a banker's concubine, of course she is happy. What did she say? While speaking, the porter had already opened the door for him. (269)

Imperial Incense Drifting Record

— Original by Princess Deling of Qing, Translated by Qin Shouou

I originally wanted to ask her for help, but unexpectedly I was subjected to a very embarrassing ridicule. I couldn't help but turn from fear to anger. I decided to ignore everything and go directly to the Empress Dowager to ask for a clear understanding of how I would be treated. At that time, I didn't have time to think, and immediately left the female officer and walked into the Empress Dowager's bedroom. Moreover, because of excessive anger, my cheeks were flushed. The Empress Dowager looked very surprised when I walked in, because she had not sent anyone to summon me: and according to the rules of the palace, I was absolutely not allowed to enter her bedroom without being summoned. Now I openly violated this rule, so she naturally felt very surprised! I didn't know what to say first, so I knelt down and bowed my head in front of her seat.

"Deling, why are you back again?" she quickly questioned me.

"Empress Dowager, I am here to kowtow to the old Buddha and apologize!" I mustered up my courage and replied to her; but my courage was limited after all, and after saying the first sentence, I couldn't help but cry. "This servant now knows that she should not have dissuaded the Empress Dowager from going to the long corridor to take a walk; it is said that in this way, I have committed a great crime, and it is said that if you don't leave, you will be beheaded, so I am anxious to apologize. Please forgive me this time!"

"Stand up!" The Empress Dowager was not angry just now, but now she was a little angry when she heard me tell the truth. She asked me questions like a pearl: "Who told you? Is it Li Lianying? Or which female official?"

"Not Chief Manager Li! It was ×× who told this servant!" I suppressed my crying and replied, "The other female officials also said that what she told me was true." (369)

World's Greatest

— Da Qian

Humans have a mind that refuses to be complacent, so the world's highest records in various fields are constantly being improved. Yesterday's best is today's second, and some may not even be able to maintain their second position. Compiling one or two examples to show the evolution of world affairs, perhaps in the blink of an eye, these records will become outdated? Alas!

World's Largest Merchant Ship The world's fastest sailing record for merchant ships has been set by the recently launched French liner Normandie, the world's largest merchant ship. The Normandie is 1,029 feet long, 128 feet wide, and 128 feet high from the keel to the top of the bridge. It has a tonnage of 79,280, surpassing all other ships in the world. About ten million rivets were used during construction, about four thousand miles of electrical wire of various thicknesses, and about fifty miles of water and steam pipes of various thicknesses. It employs 187 chefs, 628 tea servers, and 108 deck sailors. Its grand dining hall is 300 feet long, which is even more astonishing. Recently, it sailed on its maiden voyage from Southampton, England, to the United States, arriving at the Port of New York at 10:30 AM on June 3, taking four days, three hours, three minutes, and eighteen seconds, having crossed the Atlantic Ocean at an average speed of 29.68 nautical miles per hour (slightly larger than a mile, about 3.3 *li* in our country), surpassing the previous world record of 28.9 nautical miles per hour set by the Italian liner Rex (54,000 tons) departing from the Strait of Gibraltar. The fastest single day covered 748 nautical miles, averaging 31.17 nautical miles per hour, with a maximum speed reaching .9 nautical miles, which is currently the fastest record for all merchant ships in the world and exceeds the maximum speed limit of our country's trains! The Normandie's electric propulsion motors are powered by electricity generated by steam engines. The fuel for the steam engines is oil, with a steam pressure of 400 pounds per square inch and a temperature of 660 degrees Fahrenheit. This indirect power transmission system reduces the noise of the machinery. There are four generators, each with 40,000 horsepower, totaling 160,000 horsepower, which is equivalent to the power of ten average merchant ships in the Atlantic Ocean. The only ships in the world with more power are the American warships Saratoga and Lexington, aircraft carriers designed for high speed! These two ships each have 180,000 horsepower, divided into eight generators, each with 22,500 horsepower. The Normandie has four generators, so each generator is even larger than those on the aforementioned two ships. If this electricity were applied on land, it could supply the entire city of Boston, USA (population 787,271), which is also astonishing!

World's Largest Tree Among the many large trees in California, USA, the large trees in the Sequoia Grove are particularly famous. Previously, people who talked about large trees regarded the General Sherman tree in the Sequoia Grove as the world's largest tree. Geography books also often mention the name of Sequoia. Recently, Galkin and Meers, based on the large forest pointed out by Boutte, a resident of the Kaweah River, 45 years ago, engaged in exploration and actual photographic surveying. Over the years, they discovered several trees last year that were larger than the General Sherman tree. The largest one has a trunk circumference of 124 feet 6 inches at the base, exceeding the General Sherman's base circumference record of 10 feet 6 inches by more than 20 feet. It is about 4,000 years old, more than 1,000 years older than the General Sherman's 3,000 years. The title of world's tree king should belong to this newly discovered one. The treetop of this large tree has been broken off by strong winds, but it is still 200 feet tall. The trees next to it, although not as large, are up to 300 feet tall. This large tree grove is also called the Galkin Grove because Galkin and others were the first to carry out measurements. The location is also part of the Sierra Nevada mountain range in California.

World's Largest Airplane Russia has several large airplanes that can carry 40 to 50 passengers. Germany has specially built a large airplane to overwhelm them. The largest airplane currently owned by Germany is equipped with eight propellers, has a total weight of 70 tons (about 100,000 catties in our country), a wingspan of 190 feet, and can carry 70 passengers. It is named Maxon Gorky and is currently the world's largest airplane.

World's Largest Telescope The world's largest telescope is currently in the United States, with a lens diameter of 100 inches. It is located at the Mount Wilson Observatory in Pasadena, California, USA. The California Institute of Technology, located before Mount Wilson, is planning to build a 200-inch diameter large telescope, which is four times larger than the current largest telescope. Work has been underway for several years, and a 120-inch diameter test lens has now been completed. The final lens (i.e., the 200-inch diameter lens) will be about 26 inches thick and weigh about 20 tons (about 30,000 catties in our country). It has already been cast in New York and is gradually cooling down. It can be transported to the California Institute of Technology this winter for grinding. It is expected to be completed within three years. The location for installing this telescope has been selected on Mount Palomar, about 70 miles southeast of Mount Wilson. The mountain is about 6,000 feet high. The decision on this location was made after five years of investigation, comparison, and discussion by a site selection committee organized by various experts. After the telescope is completed, special attention will be paid to observing nebulae and the temperature, density, and changes of stars farther away from Earth. Based on the unprecedented light-gathering power of this telescope, it can be asserted that there will be many new cosmic discoveries.

Ministry of Education Order Instructs Nantong College to Genuinely Improve

The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 18th to the private Nantong College. The original order stated, "The Ministry has sent personnel to inspect the college. According to the submitted report, after careful review, the college aims to cultivate practical talents and has been operating for many years with some success. However, there are many areas that need improvement. The key points are highlighted as follows: (1) Although the college's land area is large, it has not been fully utilized. There is no fixed income for operating expenses, and there have been frequent deficits in recent years. The board of directors should find ways to fully develop the land to increase the foundation and raise funds to meet current needs. (2) The college's agronomy, chemistry, and dyeing and chemical engineering departments have poor equipment and few students. Given the current financial difficulties, consideration may be given to suspending them. The main courses can be incorporated into the agronomy and textile departments. Expansion can be considered when the college's funds are sufficient in the future. (3) The college's curriculum can still focus on practice. In the future, it is necessary to increase opportunities for students to conduct independent research. Teachers are dedicated and diligent in guidance. However, the few professors teaching basic subjects in the medical and textile departments should be carefully selected. (4) The college's science equipment is generally complete, but the experimental equipment for basic subjects in the medical department is particularly simple. Efforts should be made to integrate the courses with the agricultural department for utilization. The soil and fertilizer research equipment of the agricultural department and the main equipment of the dyeing and chemical engineering department of the textile department need to be enriched. Books and magazines should be selectively added. (5) The college's agricultural science buildings are old, and the medical science capacity is narrow, both of which need to be repaired or expanded. The textile testing hall of the textile department should be built and completed as soon as possible. The college is hereby ordered to comply with these instructions, genuinely improve, and report."

Ministry of Education Wireless Radio Receiver Instructor Training Class News

The Wireless Radio Receiver Instructor Training Class, organized by the Ministry of Education, is scheduled to begin tomorrow (20th) at the First Municipal Middle School on Xifu West Street in Beijing. (Guo Lianfeng, originally assigned by the Ministry of Education, resigned as director of this group due to slight physical discomfort, and the Ministry of Education has reassigned Supervisor Zhou.) Jiangsu Education Department Orders Middle Schools to Enrich Science Experiment Equipment to Enhance Students' Experimental Skills

The Jiangsu Education Department believes that most middle schools have not purchased complete equipment for physics, chemistry, and biology experiments, so students only know the theory and cannot experiment, which reduces students' experimental skills, which is extremely important for their academic future. Therefore, it specifically ordered all middle schools to enrich various scientific equipment as soon as possible. If there are economic difficulties, those that are easy to obtain can be purchased first for students to experiment with.

British Industries Association: Selection of Students to Study in the UK Held in Shanghai; Establishment of a Selection Committee Responsible for Handling Matters; Office Located at No. 17, Bund, Shanghai

The British Industries Association will continue to select Chinese students this year to intern at British factories for a period of one year, with the possibility of extension. A selection committee has been established in Shanghai to oversee the selection process. Secretary P. Campbell of the Association has already issued a recruitment notice. Those interested in applying should submit their applications to the Secretary by September 1, 1935. The number of open positions at the factories this year is no less than twelve. The products manufactured by these factories include steam boilers and cranes, telephones, radio broadcasting equipment, radios, cables, water supply equipment (meters), sluice gates, steel bridges and structural steel, pumping machines, airplanes and airplane engines, air, gas, water and steam measuring instruments, coal cutters, conveyors and electrical machinery, gears and chain drives, agricultural and ordinary machinery. Applicants should note the following requirements: (1) The age limit is 28 years old; (2) Applicants must be proficient in English and have graduated from a specialized university in China; (3) Applicants must be capable of strenuous manual labor and able to work long hours; (4) Applicants must first undergo a medical examination before being eligible for selection; (5) Applicants must be able to prepare a portion of their travel expenses and provide financial guarantees satisfactory to the Association; (6) During the internship, British manufacturers will, as usual, provide trainees with wages. Application forms can be obtained from the Secretary's Office of the Association at the British Chamber of Commerce, No. 17, Bund, Shanghai.

Guangzhou Gongping Daily Newspaper's Team Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday; Head Coach and Five Others to Arrive North Today by Eurasia Plane; Basketball and Water Polo Teams Arrive Together; Today to Visit Various Newspapers

According to Datong News Agency, the Guangzhou Gongping Daily Newspaper's investigation delegation and northern tour team, a group of fourteen people, arrived in Shanghai at around 9:00 AM yesterday and stayed at the New Asia Hotel. This reporter drove to visit and met with Mr. Peng Yingjun, captain of the newspaper's basketball team, who provided the following information:

Brief History of the Team: A Champion in Guangdong

The Guangzhou Gongping Daily Newspaper, in order to promote national sports, organized a team six years ago. After much preparation, it was finally established. Since the newspaper established various teams, it also hired basketball veteran Zhu Liaosheng as head coach, who worked tirelessly to train the team for a long time. The team has achieved great results and has become the strong force it is today. The newspaper's basketball team has won the Guangzhou Mayor's Cup and the city's open competition runner-up in both 1934 and 1935. The table tennis team also won the city championship in 1932. The water polo team is also quite strong, but the basketball team is the strongest, and is known as the basketball king of Guangzhou. The basketball and water polo teams have come to Shanghai together, but the table tennis team did not come.

Observing Sports Skills and Embarking on a Northern Expedition

The sports department of the newspaper, in order to observe sports skills, had the idea of a northern tour. At the same time, the water polo team also set off together. The members of the two teams and the members of the investigation delegation, a total of seventeen people, set off from the Taigu Sichuan Wheel on the evening of the 13th of this month and arrived in Shanghai yesterday (the 18th) morning, and stayed at the New Asia Hotel on North Sichuan Road. The team also brought many special issues of the "Northern Tour Special" to distribute to various institutions and cultural and sports organizations. As for the competition dates and assignments, the Shanghai National Sports Association will assist in the negotiations, and it will be determined after the head coach and team leader arrive in Shanghai.

Free Talk

Integrity

— Cao Juren

In Chinese history, the so-called scholar-gentlemen valued integrity above all else. Taking shortcuts and evading responsibilities were not the Confucian way. During the late Eastern Han Dynasty, when the Disaster of the Partisan Prohibitions arose, Zhang Jian was forced to flee for his life. Regardless of which family he sought refuge with, as long as they knew it was Zhang Jian, knowing that it would cause great trouble, everyone was willing to ruin their families to accommodate him. When Fan Pang was first imprisoned in the Yellow Gate Northern Temple Prison, many of his fellow prisoners were ill. Pang volunteered to be the first to be flogged and subjected to the three types of torture, his head covered and exposed on the steps. When Pang was pardoned and returned home, he was implicated in Zhang Jian's case. The court issued a decree to arrest Fan Pang and others. Wu Dao, the postal inspector, embraced the edict, closed his door, and wept on his bed. Fan Pang heard the news and knew that the postal inspector was doing it for his own sake, so he went to the county to surrender himself. Guo Yi, the county magistrate, resigned his official seal and was willing to go with Fan Pang, saying to Pang, "The world is so big, how did you come to this end?" Fan Pang said, "If I die, the great disaster will be over. How can I implicate others?" Pang said goodbye to his mother and went to prison. His mother comforted him, saying, "To die with Li Ying and Du Mi, is it not very glorious?" The Partisan Prohibitions implicated Li Ying, and someone advised Li Ying to flee. Li Ying said, "It is not difficult to deal with things, and not escaping punishment for one's crimes is the duty of a subject. I am already sixty this year, and life and death are ordained. Where can I escape to?" He went to prison and died from the toxic torture. Those implicated in the Partisan Prohibitions, including their students, former officials, and their fathers and brothers, were all on the list of prohibitions. Jing Yi of Shu County had his son become a disciple of Li Ying. Because there was no official record, he was exempt from the prohibitions. Jing Yi voluntarily requested to be dismissed from office, saying, "Because I admired Li Ying's character, I asked my son to follow him. How can I be complacent just because his name was omitted from the list?" From these various instances, one can imagine the situation at that time, where scholar-gentlemen valued integrity, disregarded their lives, and were unwilling to evade responsibilities and take shortcuts.

When misfortune strikes, many relatives and friends will avoid suspicion and disaster. However, according to Confucian principles, avoiding suspicion and disaster is also inappropriate. Kong Rong was upright and often clashed with Cao Cao. His friend Zhi Xi often advised Rong to be wise and protect himself. Later, Kong Rong was killed by Cao Cao, and his body was displayed in Xuxia, but no one dared to collect it. Zhi Xi went to caress the body and wept bitterly, disregarding being detained by Cao Huan. Similarly, when Zhang Jian fled to the State of Lu because of the Partisan Prohibitions, he wanted to seek refuge with Kong Bao. It happened that Kong Bao was not at home, but Kong Rong, who was only sixteen years old, took him in without authorization. Later, the matter was revealed, and Bao and Rong were both arrested and sent to prison. Kong Rong stepped forward and said, "I was the one who took in Zhang Jian. Please punish me!" Kong Bao said, "Zhang Jian came to me, and it has nothing to do with my younger brother. Please punish me!" The officials could not decide for a long time, so they had to ask their mother for her opinion. The mother said, "I am the head of the family, and I am responsible. Please punish me!" The whole family struggled to die, and even the county could not decide. When we look at this spirit of sacrificing oneself for righteousness, it still inspires us thousands of years later. No wonder it shook the hearts of ordinary people at that time, and everyone wanted to hone their integrity!

"The greatest sorrow is the death of the heart." If everyone considers it advantageous to take shortcuts and evade responsibilities, then every Chinese scholar will become a "traitor"! As the saying of "propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame" is flourishing, I hope that the people of our country will pay attention to the word "shame" and value "integrity" above all else.

Large Fried Dough Sticks (You Tiao)

— Qin Wen

The year my nephew was born, my sister-in-law was teaching. If she resigned to breastfeed herself, the living expenses would not be enough. After calculating, she thought it was better to hire a wet nurse, although she knew it was not very appropriate, she had no choice but to do it.

The wet nurse was very diligent and saved even more money. In the two years, she didn't seem to have exchanged her formal salary of one yuan. Since she became a wet nurse, the money her husband sent home every month was enough to cover the children fostered in the neighbors. Her salary was saved in full. When the nephew was weaned, because of her good credit, she borrowed dozens of dollars more. Her husband was originally from a tofu-making family, so they opened a small tofu shop together. The business was not bad. They took back the children, reunited the family, and the man made the tofu and the woman sold it. It was indeed envious - this was two years ago.

Unexpectedly, over the past year or so, business has gradually become sluggish. It was not because the tofu was made badly, nor was it because she offended any customers. It was just that radishes and cabbages were too cheap. Two or three copper coins could buy a large pile, and even pork was six or seven catties for one yuan. Rent and taxes were still high, but tofu could not be reduced in price. Unless it's a vegetarian dish, tofu is not considered anything. Who would be willing to pay a high price to buy this kind of thing to eat? In order to maintain the business, the wet nurse's tofu shop started selling fried stinky tofu. Although it was a small supplement, the sales of tofu became worse and worse, and it was still not enough to make ends meet, so they started selling fried dough sticks (you tiao).

The nephew could already walk, but the family situation became more and more dismal, so they simply ate lunch boxes: breakfast was porridge, with a plate of fried dough sticks, which were cut into very small pieces. The nephew was not satisfied and often clamored to go to the wet nurse's to eat whole fried dough sticks.

This day there was no sun, nor was it raining. Although it was early summer, it was as gloomy as late autumn. It was very stuffy indoors, so my sister-in-law took her nephew for a walk. I knew that once they went out, they would always go to the wet nurse's tofu shop for a turn, and I happened to meet them at the door on their way back.

"Did you eat fried dough sticks?" I asked casually.

"There are only two large fried dough sticks!" My sister-in-law replied angrily.

"Two, isn't that enough?"

"That's really a fried dough stick, it's two pieces of wood, it looks like two large fried dough sticks, crossed and nailed to the front of the shop, probably because of too much debt, it was sealed!"

"Couldn't see them," my sister-in-law said excitedly, "Don't know where they went, maybe they were held in court."

The nephew had already walked into the room, and my sister-in-law was still standing blankly at the entrance, looking very touched. She really had deep sympathy for the wet nurse, but what's the use of that? Everyone understood early on that the debt was growing day by day, which was not a solution, but there was no way to stop the long-term decline in the price of radishes and cabbages - farmers carried a heavy burden, but they could only sell them for a few dozen copper coins. It was difficult enough to plant and work hard, and the reward was only a very small amount.

In fact, my sister-in-law herself was not to be lamented. After being the principal of a municipal elementary school for many years, she had only been a nanny for her own children for two years. She couldn't do it well because she had to save money on food and clothing!

Lunch

— Written by Chen Jingsheng

Condolences for a Friend Who Died of Lovesickness

— Shen Shengshi

A fragile dream, like a soap bubble bursting,

You took it so seriously.

I can't think of the best words

To comfort your infatuated soul.

The world is not as innocent as you imagined;

Pure love has long fallen into hardship.

Only gold can hold onto beautiful dreams.

All the beauty is just fabricated lies.

Life is not a smooth circle;

Not every dream comes true according to your wishes.

What you yearn for often slips through your fingers,

And the most vexing things are chained to your ankles for life,

Not easily loosened until death.

Only the fragile dreams you clung to,

Were like bubbles, shattered by a single gust of wind.

Now you have entered the dark world.

Death is life's greatest rest.

The wild grass and idle flowers on the grave path

May still disturb your soul.

On stormy, rainy nights,

There may be a regret knocking on your frozen heart.

Mirror

— Luo Jia

Usually, I don't pay much attention to my clothes, and I don't even care about the oil on my face or my unkempt beard. Every morning, before I can carefully wipe away the overnight grime, there are already things waiting for me to do. Because of this hasty grooming, it's easy to leave some dirt on my face. My face isn't naturally fair, so any dirt left uncleaned makes my complexion dull and lifeless. If at this moment I suddenly thought of wanting to know something about the future and went to visit an old fortune teller, then what he would tell me would definitely be, "Your luck is not good this year!" Although, someone as busy with the present as I am doesn't have the refined leisure to visit fortune tellers!

Perhaps some might say that "sloppy appearance" is a quirk of scholars, but this saying has no effect on me at all, because I am neither a scholar nor do I aspire to be one, so why would I want to imitate famous scholars and feign elegance? And how dare I! In fact, if someone said I was ashamed, that might be somewhat reasonable. For the sake of living, I've had to become too lazy to bother with things like grooming! Once ashamed, it becomes a habit, and I can no longer change it.

It was probably one day in May when I went to visit a friend. It so happened that in my friend's parlor, there were two young ladies who were also guests, just like me. When I walked into the parlor, I found that these two young ladies were staring at me with an expression as if they wanted to laugh but couldn't, which made me very embarrassed! Because I rarely socialize with the opposite sex in my life. But I always thought that these two young ladies were probably laughing at my tattered long gown, and I was a little disdainful of them in my heart. However, my friend quietly called me into his bedroom and told me that there was a smudge of ink on my face. Then I suddenly understood the reason why the two young ladies were laughing at me; at the same time, I also felt the need for a mirror! If I had looked in the mirror when I went out, then I could have avoided being laughed at by the young ladies.

Because I couldn't forget the young ladies' mockery, I resolved to buy a mirror, and the mirror was finally bought! This mirror is very beautiful, not to mention the crystal-clear and shiny surface; the pearly and jade-colored, goose-yellow bakelite frame alone is enough for me to ponder and applaud! So, I reverently placed it on my desk, thinking that this mirror would help me pay attention to news of my youth!

Because of premature maturity, I became a melancholic young man—no, an old young man! Yes, I think the phrase "old young man" is the most suitable for my elegant self-description. Since I had a mirror, I had even clearer evidence. Isn't that so? Every time I look at myself in the mirror, I often can't believe that the shadow in the mirror is me! If it is me, then I want to ask, where is my youth? Where is my youth? Could it be that my youth has withered silently without leaving a trace? Naturally, when a person discovers that their youth has withered silently, what kind of words should be used to describe that person's sadness in the most accurate way? However, I now have only a heart of twenty! Why is my face so old? Why are there already indelible wrinkles on my forehead? Moreover, why has the lively smile of my youth been replaced by a kind of silence that knows the ways of the world? Ah! If I indulge in my feelings and keep thinking about it, I will become an artist! Life, life, life devoured my youth, life painted over the radiance of youth on my face, terrible life!

To avoid my own sadness, I threw the mirror into the corner of the room, letting dust and cobwebs bury it!

I Love Solitude

— Luo Hong

Because I am exhausted from being worn down by life, because my heart has been pricked by the thorns around me, I have come to love solitude even more lately. Now, I understand how easily a pure heart can be damaged, and how easily courage to move forward can be blocked by the environment. If you act with uprightness and give fairness to others, someone will surely laugh at your foolishness openly and sabotage you secretly. If you kindly do something or say a word for others, the result will be their malice. Even if you read a book for yourself, someone will laugh at you and spread rumors. So, a pure heart slowly becomes depressed, surrounded by this filthy air. Therefore, in the whirlpool of crowds, I deeply feel loneliness; the meaning of this loneliness buries my youthful and active heart in a gloomy cellar.

Around me, there is no hope, no joy, not even friendship. When I laugh, the iron palm of sorrow crushes me; when I muster courage, disappointment blocks me; so, in the end, I only get loneliness.

I love solitude, to have a little leisure in life, to think alone about the past and the future, which is much more interesting than finding a friend to say many irrelevant and boring things; or to be alone in a pile of books, reading freely, crying and laughing with the characters in the book, with no one to interfere with you, which is much better than listening to others' scolding.

I am not learning from the elegant scholars of ancient and modern times, deliberately avoiding the crowd and singing high-pitched tunes alone. I just want to silently endure the pain and silently put my heart in a place with more moonlight. The victory achieved by striving in solitude is not worth exaggerating, and the failure in solitude is not enough to make courage completely disappear.

A friend wrote to me and said: "Why are you so silent? Won't you resist the environment?..." This friend also wrote many words of concern for me, but I cannot accept her kindness. I really want to laugh at my friend for being too naive. She doesn't yet know how my innocent heart, like hers, has been damaged.

I wish that this unfortunate fate of mine would spend my life steadily in solitude.

University Days (26)

— From the German of Storm, translated by Chen Yinshi

Before he finished speaking, I had already walked to the desk and counted a handful of gold coins onto the table. "Is that enough, Christoph?"

"I thank you, Philip." He carefully put the gold coins into his money bag, which already had many gold and silver coins in it. Only then did I notice that he was standing in front of me wearing his black Sunday clothes.

"You've put on your formal dress," I asked, "where have you been just now?"

"This..." he said, thoughtfully rubbing his broad forehead with his hand, "I went to the police station!"

"Have you gotten your passport yet?"

"Yes, I even have my letter of resignation."

I stared at him with a questioning look.

"It's because of that silly thing at the dance hall."

Suddenly, my mind lit up. "So that's it! So you're the one?" I asked him; "Look at me, I didn't even think it was you!"

"I was indeed there, Philip."

"Was Rena Li with you?"

He nodded.

"So you gave the 'Count' a beating?"

A smile of revenge appeared on his lips. "They say I hit him," he replied.

The old nemesis in the student world said this with a satisfied tone, which made me have no doubt about the matter.

I couldn't help but laugh out loud. "Tell me! How did that happen?"

"This..., Philip! Don't you already know I went with Rena Li?"

"Did you two make an appointment to go together?"

"That's how it happened." he replied. "She is a very talented person, and after Aunt's death she can get a small estate."

I looked at him with a smile. "Christoph," I said, "She is usually very good; it's just you, you are usually not so easy to hit people!" He stared ahead for a while. "I was also baffled," he said, "We were standing in line, Nali and I, —I went there just to help her interest—the pale-faced tall guy came, he had often stared at her, and at this time he said a few words in a low voice to another person, and he wanted to dance with her specially regardless of the order.

"Then wasn't he too rude to your dance partner?"

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

The Problem of Water Conservancy Construction Under Severe Floods

— Xing An

Recently, the Yangtze River, Yellow River, Qiantang River, and the Three Rivers of Guangdong Province have all reported a surge in water levels. Many embankments and dikes along the rivers have been destroyed, and floods have become a disaster. Although the authorities of various provinces have been actively carrying out disaster relief and flood prevention work, the water of the rivers is surging fiercely, and the dangerous situation is increasing day by day. The terror of the national flood disaster of 1931 has reappeared today. China, which is deeply troubled by foreign aggression, will suffer another blow, and the future national economy and people's livelihood will be even more unimaginable.

Floods have been a disaster since ancient times. Our country's authorities have neither made a fundamental plan for water control, nor can they only panic and do their best when threatened by major floods each time. This is the only method of water control throughout history. The great flood of 1931 gave us a major warning. If the Chinese people can learn from this severe injury and urgently take precautions, today's disasters, if they cannot be avoided, will not be so widespread. Therefore, the dangerousness of this flood is not the result of the past water control policies of following the old ways and doing nothing.

Floods are originally a natural disaster, but human power can overcome nature. As long as prevention is appropriate, it is not difficult to overcome. However, our country adopts a method of treating the head when the head hurts and treating the feet when the feet hurt for flood prevention work. Never think about it from the root and make a permanent plan.

However, can fundamental water control be allowed by our country's economic strength today? According to the investigation of many foreign water conservancy experts, the fundamental method of preventing the floods of the Yangtze River and Yellow River is not in raising the dikes, but in the construction of water conservancy. Increasing the dikes is not only not a way to prevent flooding, but once the water collapses, the disaster will be even more dangerous. However, water conservancy construction must raise huge funds to purchase water conservancy machinery for implementation. At this time of national poverty and people's poverty, our country has no such ability. Recently, a reporter from the Central News Agency visited a foreign water conservancy expert to inquire about water control methods. According to the discussion, he believes that the method of raising funds to purchase machines for water control is not suitable for the current China. But he believes that China's hoes and plows and other agricultural tools can be used as good machines for water control. If the authorities of various provinces in China can supervise the hardworking Chinese people to use their hoes and plows and other agricultural tools to open tributaries on both sides of the river. At the same time, the water conservancy organs should abandon their work of raising the dikes and focus on the dredging of the waterways. Then not only can floods be avoided, but also river water can be diverted to irrigate fields, which is a gain in many ways. We are not water conservancy experts, and we know nothing about water conservancy construction. However, according to the water conservancy expert, the above-mentioned opinions are confident enough for the Chinese water conservancy authorities to study. I hope the Chinese people will pay attention to it.

Jealousy

— Tuo Ren

"Miss Lan's Eyes"—an ear-piercing name rushed into the director's ears. He darted a sharp, fire-spewing glance at the clerk, his eyes fixed unmovingly on the clerk's face. The sudden stare made the clerk feel a terrifying threat, but he couldn't escape. He had no choice but to say, swallowing his pride, "Director, I say, hurry up and bring Miss Lan over. It'll save you from running back and forth every day."

The clerk stammered out these words, thinking that he had certainly hit the director's secret heart this time! But unexpectedly, the director still didn't say a word, his eyes still fixed on the clerk's face. At this point, the clerk also felt his own failure, felt awkward, and he fell silent as well.

After a dozen minutes of silence, the clerk reached out on the desk and groped for a cigar, offering it to the director, who was lying on the sofa, while he himself held a cigarette. So the two temporarily used smoking to replace the silence. Finally, the director opened his mouth and said,

"You would never think that from last night until now, I haven't been able to solve a problem."

After the director finished speaking, his eyes fixed on the clerk's face again. The clerk, who was good at flattery and known to be very good at thinking up cunning and insidious things, thought it was time to speak. So he said with a smile,

"Director, how could someone like you have any problems that are difficult to solve? I've already planned out that sum of money, everything is no problem. According to my calculations, every month... Humph, every month we should have at least five or six thousand, and..."

The clerk went on and on, but the director became impatient. He interrupted the clerk and said, no longer letting him go on,

"That's not it, you know? That hateful guy, I..."

The clerk knew he had said the wrong thing and immediately changed his tone, asking,

"Who? Is someone opposing you, Director? Is it that the chairman of the chamber of commerce doesn't approve of drawing construction fees? Or... Ah! How hateful! Director, you don't need to worry about these things!"

Every year, the clerk was responsible for planning some money matters for the director. All the director's difficult matters were nothing more than these, so he paid attention only to these issues. But the director spoke out himself.

"Damn it, that guy Huang Shiqi, I must deal with him..." He paused, took a puff of his cigar, and said again, "Doesn't he know that I'm going to marry Lan Mei next month? He, humph, still wants to fool around. You think, last night he even went to her place."

These sudden words stunned the clerk. This was truly unexpected. It turned out that the director was troubled by something that no amount of searching would uncover in his entire brain. He was silent for a few minutes before saying to the director,

"So... How about Miss Lan? That guy Huang Shiqi is really no good!"

"Her? What about her? I'm willing to marry her, wouldn't she be willing? But that guy Huang Shiqi must be dealt with a bit!"

After hearing the director's answer, the clerk lowered his head, silently smoking his cigarette. The clerk, who was specialized at thinking of cunning and insidious things, could only be silent on this matter. He searched his heart, mind, gut—every clever part of him. After a quarter of an hour, he looked at the director very seriously and said,

"The best way to deal with him is to dismiss him, but the reason must be grand, that is, 'secretly consorting with prostitutes.' But, I'm afraid that's too easy on him."

After hearing the clerk use the crime of "secretly consorting with prostitutes" on Huang Shiqi, the director thought it was not bad. But he also thought that this was still too light of a punishment. So the anger on the director's face gradually faded, and he said to the clerk with a smile,

"You're really smart. This method is very good. Do it immediately. Write a notice and a letter of dismissal!"

Having received the answer, a victorious smile floated on the clerk's cunning and insidious face.

So everything in the director's office returned to silence, with only the sound of the clerk writing the notice and official letter on the desk resonating for a long time. (End)

Small Chronicle of the Customs of the Bai Yi

— Dan Er

The Bai Yi people live on the edge of the Chinese begonia leaf. They are considered part of China and should be Chinese people; however, the old habit of Chinese people has not yet been removed, and they are called Yi, one of the "Four Barbarians," so they are called Bai Yi. And most people, of course, do not know of the existence of such people.

They live in the border area of Yunnan Province, mostly in the mountain valleys and streams between the continuous mountains. To the west, they adjoin Myanmar, and to the south, they border Annam. The Water Bai Yi mostly live by the water, and the Dry Bai Yi live entirely on the mountains.

The Water Bai Yi, who live by the water, have very fair and delicate complexions, and are leisurely and isolated, growing alone in the tranquil and elegant landscape paintings of the beautiful nature. People are especially detached and carefree. The bamboo forest by the water rustles, ceaselessly playing celestial music in the gentle southern breeze. Here, dense bamboo forests are everywhere. The houses of the Bai Yi people are not like our tall and heavy gray earth houses, but are all bamboo buildings built with bamboo. Below the mountains and above the water, rows of bamboo buildings are extremely harmonious with the natural landscape. When the wind sweeps through the mountains and forests and the blue waves, their bamboo buildings seem to dance lightly, as leisurely as living bamboo clumps and grasses, making people feel inexplicably cheerful.

Page 20

Moving, like the overflowing spring tide, like the free-flowing blue waves, spreading and surging.

The bamboo buildings are divided into two floors, and the exterior is very delicate and lovely. The upper floor is inhabited by the Bai Yi, and although it is simple, it is exceptionally plain and natural. They are particularly particular about cleanliness. Before and after meals, a basin of clean cold water must be placed on the table, and they must wash their hands before eating. The chopsticks are local bamboo chopsticks, and they are discarded after each use, with new ones replaced each time. This is very similar to the customs of civilized people; however, the lower floor of the bamboo building is entirely a den for livestock, raising various kinds of domestic animals, with animal manure and weeds scattered everywhere. The upper and lower floors are two completely different worlds.

Since ancient times, the people of Yunnan have regarded them as barbarians, not intermarrying with them, and rarely interacting with them. Of course, it is very difficult to find those who speak Chinese and know Chinese characters; however, the Chinese are afraid of going far, and gradually they are more fluent in foreign languages such as English and French. Their clothing has also become increasingly Westernized, and they are much more modern than the Yunnan people who call them barbarians. Many women are as Westernized as those fashionable women in Shanghai.

Foreign missionaries not only come to cities with convenient transportation to spread the gospel of God, but their footprints can also be found in the dwellings of the Bai Yi, which are so remote that even we Chinese people do not know about them.

Therefore, those near Myanmar are more assimilated by the British, and those near Annam are more assimilated by the French. Everything is Yi but Westernized, and they are even more distant from the owner of the Chinese begonia leaf.

They love singing and dancing the most. Although the musical instruments are simple and the dances are mostly of the rough-line type, their innocence, liveliness, and natural enthusiasm are extremely capable of expressing their unique national character. However, the influence of Western forces is becoming more and more pervasive, and even singing and dancing are becoming more Westernized.

Mountain songs are very intoxicating folk poems of the Bai Yi people. When I traveled through the bamboo forests of the Bai Yi, although I did not know their meaning, the especially light, clear, sincere, and natural tones were very pleasant to hear. Now is the time of the scorching heat of summer in the big cities, and recalling the mountains and waters of the clear, cool, and refreshing Bai Yi places makes people naturally intoxicated in the dreams of memory.

The Dry Bai Yi have a less leisurely life than the Water Bai Yi. They all live in the mountains, and their products are not as abundant as those of the Water Bai Yi, so they have developed a very hardworking nature and a spirit of life that is completely different from that of modern society. Their national character is not as barbaric as the Chinese call them Yi. Their population accounts for about one-tenth or two-tenths of Yunnan, but they are all "Westernizing." Although they live on the edge of the Chinese begonia leaf, they are gradually changing color, and are still unknown to the owner of the Chinese begonia leaf.

Women

— Zhen Huan

It's getting dark!

The vast twilight brings a deepening gloom.

Knife-scarred A Lin staggered out of the small tavern by the sharp bend, where he had bought cigarettes and filled his belly with hot "Green Bean Brew." His two heavy, limp legs struggled to support his crooked upper body, swaying and dragging his unsteady, sluggish steps. The sparse streetlights, one after another, emitted faint light, the darkness often causing him to brush against the low eaves of the houses.

Turning a corner and passing through the Jin Family Archway, he would be at the edge of the city. In the lonely, desolate outskirts, covered with a withered yellow straw roof, that was his home!

"Open the door!" he called out in a hoarse voice:

"Oh! Is that Uncle A Lin?" a delicate, clear voice of a woman squeezed through the door crack:

Then, with a creak, the door opened! A Lin, carrying a fiery, strong smell of "Green Bean Brew," rushed in with the night wind.

"Oh dear, the lamp almost blew out!" the woman's voice was as weak as a soft catkin:

"Th... Thank you, Sister-in-law," A Lin's tongue felt sluggish and strange. His drunken eyes, filled with red veins, rolled over the woman's loosely buttoned cotton jacket, and an unavoidable, base thought swirled in his confused mind like a rising wave.

"This woman is quite pretty!" A smile, sparingly, slipped across the corner of his mouth, but after a moment, as if remembering something, he fell silent!

(A faint shadow, like a wisp of distant rosy clouds, floated past. In a certain year when he was accustomed to a leisurely life wandering around Xinglong Town, during the flowering of the pomegranates, he met Big-eyed Shun Sheng, who had come from × Port to escape trouble, and his young wife. Because they were both secretly engaged in smuggling, the two of them knelt before the Bodhisattva, lit three thin incense sticks, and kowtowed loudly. - Of course, Shun Sheng's young wife addressed A Lin as "Brother" and respected him as "Sister-in-law." But Shun Sheng, that unlucky fellow, had his business exposed and was arrested by men sent from the magistrate's office, who put him in shackles. The county magistrate tried him for one year and eight months. But this woman, in the end, under A Lin's righteous attitude, was taken into his home. The people in the town all praised A Lin for being a man of honor and loyalty!)

"Ah! Uncle A Lin, you're drunk again!" The light from the woman's lamp shone on A Lin's flushed face, which was in a trance.

"Heh... drunk again, good Sister-in-law, I... A Lin misses you so much!" A Lin's lips trembled, causing his entire body to shiver violently!

"What's this! Uncle A Lin, are you talking nonsense in your drunken stupor?" The woman panicked, her eyes widening in surprise.

"Good Sister-in-law, I'm not talking nonsense in my drunken stupor! I want to have some fun with you!"

"Humph! You should think about your Brother!"

"Oh! Shun Sheng? He's in jail! Good... Sister-in-law, you... agree, won't you!" A Lin's arms lunged toward the woman's chest like lightning.

"Help...!" The lamp in the woman's hand was smashed on the ground, her two tender, plump arms were tightly gripped by A Lin! Overwhelmed by the authority of violence and contempt, she wearily succumbed to A Lin's panting movements!

The lamp, knocked over by A Lin's arm onto a pile of dry straw, at this moment, the thick and thin, lively, golden snake-like flames, immediately spread throughout the house.

Terror awakened A Lin's confused intoxication! He didn't care about the body beside him that had suffered cruel manipulation, and at the same time he abandoned the approaching death, braving the thick smoke and fleeing!

Poor woman, she was half-paralyzed in a coma, as if her soul had disappeared! In an instant, she was engulfed in the melody of the raging fire, crackling and sizzling as she burned into a black mass!

The next day, news of A Lin's death spread throughout the town, and the scene of the fire was crowded with people, but they all forgot that the corpse was Shun Sheng's young wife!

Lu Fengxiang Lu Xiaoxiang The Tale of the White Snake

Fu Xing (920) 2:00 PM to 3:00 PM

Opening piece "Xiao Xiang Night Rain"

The smoke swirls, shrouding the curtained room. The moon is hazy, its light dim and yellow. A misty, misty Xiao Xiang Lodge. A bleak, bleak few windows with emerald silk. A whistling, whistling thousand bamboo canes. Green, green several slender crabapple branches. A weary, weary, melancholy woman. Cold and lonely, two small plum blossoms. Only to see her, a thin, thin, thin silk dress. Yellow and gaunt, yellow, a face like a yellow flower. Her eyes drowsy, drowsy, sorrow adding to her thoughts. Her eyebrows furrowed, furrowed, furrowed, her eyebrows filled with hatred. Quietly, quietly, she sits on the Xiang Fei couch. Softly, softly, she leans on the ivory bed. A dimly, dimly lit, half-burnt candle. A cold, icy, half cup of decocted medicine. Pitiable, panting. Her heart wavering. Coughing sounds. Tears welling up. Blood stains moistening her thin silk skirt. Earnestly, earnestly, her feelings uneasy. Sighing again and again, her sighs mournful. Pitiful, leaving, leaving, separating from her homeland. Alone, alone, her traces residing in a foreign land. The road is long, the cloud journey thousands of miles apart. White, white, unable to see her old home. Vaguely, vaguely afraid of nearing the Yellow Springs. Better to ask, ask, to go to meet the Impermanence sooner. See her, her spirit distracted, ten thousand thoughts empty. Alone, all things are vicissitudes. Only to see that, the night is deep, the night is dismal. Sounds silent, sadness increases. Only to hear, the wind rustling, rustling, the wind cold and harsh. Rain drizzling, drizzling, the rain heavy. Drip, drip, the bronze water clock leaks endlessly. Clang, clang, the iron horse rings coldly. Thump, thump, the wind moves the curtain hook. Pattering, pattering, raindrops hit the cold window. Ding-dang-dang, the bell tolls three times. Boom, boom, the watchtower strikes the fifth watch. That concubine, cold, cold, unable to withstand the cold wind. The night is long, the night rain breaks her heart. From then on, sick, sick, the disease enters the marrow.

Cheng Fangzhou Li Liansun Mao Jiashu

Hua Mei (1060) 3:00 PM to 3:30 PM

Opening piece "Young Wife Missing Her Husband"

Continuous wind and rain beat against the silk window. A young woman in her boudoir. The cuckoo cries sadly. Moved by her heart, tears welling up. Only to see that, the bright moon hangs in the sky, as clear as possible. Causing her to see the bright moon and feel even more heartbroken. All day long she misses her husband. Mournfully guarding the ivory bed. She hates her husband, how difficult it is to part with him. Saying that he would return home in less than half a year. Time passes easily, hiring people to grow old. A year alone in the quilt, doubly mournful. Surely you, by nature, are amorous and greedy for beautiful women. In brothels, you have made a new pair of amorous lovebirds. Soft jade and warm fragrance delay your future. Laughing happily all day, forgetting your wife. Or perhaps you have become acquainted with a woman of beautiful face and moonlike appearance, a woman of passionate feelings. Enjoying yourself in a foreign land. Nearly a year has passed without news. Few discuss the matters in my heart. I am diligent in household affairs morning and night. I miss my husband until the fifth watch every night. Spring breezes and autumn moons pass easily. When people grow old and their beauty fades, their hearts are most wounded. I am resentful that you have no thought of home. The joy of the boudoir is just a dream. Do not mention good flowers and a full moon. The flowing water heartlessly secretly wounds itself. I, when I think of sad things. I am even more heartbroken in the sound of the wind and rain. The cuckoo cries continuously, filled with hatred.

Movie News

Fragments from Diantong

Yuan Muzhi's "Cityscape" will gather all the characteristics of the city, and pay more attention to civic sports. The other day, on the French Republic Memorial Day, a temporary location team was formed to go to the French Park to capture the lanterns, arches and the marching crowds in front.

The Diantong basketball team had a friendly match with the Shanghai Magnesium team at the Yanshupu Road Fire Brigade cement court, resulting in a score of 21 to 16, with Diantong winning.

Miss Wang Ying recently bought many exquisite sofa beds, writing desks, etc., and has moved into the Diantong actress dormitory.

Diantong photographer Yang Longming has a deep understanding of photochemistry. He also arranges the lighting very appropriately on the set on weekdays. It is expected that the photography of "Freedom God" will have very good results.

Shi Chao, a newcomer in "Freedom God," has achieved such results on his first time on the silver screen, and Diantong attaches great importance to him.

Further News on the Re-performance of "Nora"

In the re-performance of "Nora," because Wei Heling, who played the role of Dr. Nan Hai, returned to his hometown due to his mother's illness, the role has now been invited to be played by Zheng Junli of Lianhua Company. Zheng has always been extremely cautious in his acting. In addition to stepping up rehearsals, he immediately discusses the personality of Nan Hai and his position in the play with others whenever he has time. In the future performances, the acting is bound to have a unique place. It is also heard that after the last public performance, many people from the academic community wrote to say that the ticket prices were too high, and they were unable to appreciate it. This time, a special kind of low-priced ticket for the academic community is set up to make up for the regrets of the last time. The location of the public performance has been decided as Lake Society, and the date has been decided as the 21st of this month. Seat tickets have now begun to be sold. Simalu Modern Bookstore, Shanghai Magazine Company, China Magazine Company, Lequn Magazine Company, Times Bookstore, and Xiahui Road Women's Bookstore are all acting as agents.

Fragments from Lianhua

Cai Chusheng's new work after "New Woman," the script has been completed and will be sent to Beijing for registration soon. The male lead is set to be Zheng Junli and Ge Zuo, and the female lead is planned to be played by Li Zhuozhu.

The "Wild Goose" song sung by Wang Renmei in her recent work "Little Angel" has been recorded by Baidai Company with excellent results.

Ma Xuwibang's "Wild Geese Descending on the Cold River" is working extremely intensely. This play stars Chen Yanyan, so Chen has been extremely busy on the set recently.

Lianhua's sound film "Waves Washing Sand" this year is set to star Jin Yan and Zhang Zhizhi. Screenwriter and director Wu Yonggang is now working on the scenes, and will be going to Qingdao to capture location shots in the near future.

Wan Zuozhi, the protagonist of "Little Angel," and Yin Xiucen, the fattest man in China, are learning to swim. Ge could not swim, so he laid prone on Yin's back, his form resembling a monkey riding an elephant across the river in "Tarzan Couple."

A secret screening of "The Great Road" has taken place. According to viewers' news: "This film is more realistic than the previously sensational 'Humanity,' depicting human love to its peak. There is no doubt that it will win the sympathy of the general audience when it is released later."

Li Keng's "Old Man" Song

Since "Goddess," our little star Li Keng has not had any new works released, and his many viewers are naturally looking forward to it.

"The Great Road" is his recent work, and only one location shot is missing for the entire play to be completed successfully. Li Keng plays Zheng Junli in his childhood here. The plays he performed were all very important, and he achieved unprecedented success.

The film he is preparing to star in is "Childhood China," which is a long-promoted children's epic. This film is entirely dialogue and singing, and is directed by Fei Mu.

Because he was filming a sound film, Li Keng had already learned Mandarin very well. Now he has also hired a teacher to start learning to sing. Recently, Baidai Company has recorded the "Old Man" song into a record, and this record will be published soon. We believe this record will be very popular.
